===== START: src/app/(public)/results/page.tsx =====
     1	"use client";
     2	
     3	import Link from "next/link";
     4	import { useRouter } from "next/navigation";
     5	import { PublicHeader } from "@/components/public/public-header";
     6	import { PublicFooter } from "@/components/public/public-footer";
     7	import { readyPackages } from "@/lib/mock/bangkok-builder-data";
     8	import { getRecommendedPackages } from "@/lib/helpers/recommendation";
     9	import { useTripBuilderStore } from "@/store/useTripBuilderStore";
    10	
    11	export default function ResultsPage() {
    12	  const router = useRouter();
    13	
    14	  const destination = useTripBuilderStore((state) => state.destination);
    15	  const segments = useTripBuilderStore((state) => state.segments);
    16	  const adults = useTripBuilderStore((state) => state.adults);
    17	  const children = useTripBuilderStore((state) => state.children);
    18	  const budget = useTripBuilderStore((state) => state.budget);
    19	  const travelStyle = useTripBuilderStore((state) => state.travelStyle);
    20	  const selectedPackageId = useTripBuilderStore((state) => state.selectedPackageId);
    21	  const selectPackage = useTripBuilderStore((state) => state.selectPackage);
    22	
    23	  const tripLabel = segments
    24	    .map((segment) => segment.city)
    25	    .filter(Boolean)
    26	    .join(" → ");
    27	
    28	  const recommendedPackages = getRecommendedPackages(
    29	    readyPackages.map((item, index) => ({
    30	      id: item.id,
    31	      title: item.title,
    32	      basePrice: item.price,
    33	      popularityScore: index === 0 ? 10 : 7 - index,
    34	      marginScore: item.hotelCategory === "4 Star" ? 8 : 7,
    35	      budgetFitScore:
    36	        budget === "Luxury"
    37	          ? item.price >= 40000
    38	            ? 9
    39	            : 5
    40	          : budget === "Premium"
    41	          ? item.price >= 30000 && item.price < 50000
    42	            ? 9
    43	            : 6
    44	          : budget === "Economy"
    45	          ? item.price < 32000
    46	            ? 9
    47	            : 5
    48	          : 8,
    49	      tripMoodFitScore:
    50	        travelStyle === "Mixed"
    51	          ? 8
    52	          : item.title.toLowerCase().includes(travelStyle.toLowerCase().split(" ")[0])
    53	          ? 9
    54	          : 6,
    55	      recommendedLabel: item.tag,
    56	    }))
    57	      .map((scored) => {
    58	        const original = readyPackages.find((pkg) => pkg.id === scored.id)!;
    59	        return {
    60	          ...original,
    61	          score: scored,
    62	        };
    63	      })
    64	      .sort((a, b) => {
    65	        const aScore =
    66	          (a.score.popularityScore || 0) +
    67	          (a.score.marginScore || 0) +
    68	          (a.score.budgetFitScore || 0) +
    69	          (a.score.tripMoodFitScore || 0);
    70	        const bScore =
    71	          (b.score.popularityScore || 0) +
    72	          (b.score.marginScore || 0) +
    73	          (b.score.budgetFitScore || 0) +
    74	          (b.score.tripMoodFitScore || 0);
    75	
    76	        return bScore - aScore;
    77	      })
    78	      .map((item) => item)
    79	  );
    80	
    81	  function handlePackageSelect(item: (typeof readyPackages)[number]) {
    82	    selectPackage({
    83	      selectedPackageId: item.id,
    84	      selectedPackageTitle: item.title,
    85	      selectedPackagePrice: item.price,
    86	    });
    87	
    88	    router.push("/customize");
    89	  }
    90	
    91	  return (
    92	    <div className="min-h-screen bg-[linear-gradient(180deg,#f8fbff_0%,#f8fafc_35%,#ffffff_100%)]">
    93	      <PublicHeader />
    94	
    95	      <main>
    96	        <section className="border-b border-slate-200/70 bg-white/60">
    97	          <div className="mx-auto max-w-7xl px-4 py-12 sm:px-6 lg:px-8">
    98	            <div className="rounded-[36px] border border-slate-200 bg-white p-6 shadow-[0_20px_70px_rgba(15,23,42,0.05)]">
    99	              <div className="flex flex-wrap items-center justify-between gap-4">
   100	                <div>
   101	                  <p className="text-sm font-medium text-sky-700">Results</p>
   102	                  <h1 className="mt-2 text-3xl font-semibold text-slate-950 sm:text-4xl">
   103	                    Curated options for your {destination} trip
   104	                  </h1>
   105	                  <p className="mt-3 text-sm text-slate-600">
   106	                    {tripLabel || destination} • {adults} Adults
   107	                    {children ? `, ${children} Children` : ""} • {travelStyle}
   108	                  </p>
   109	                </div>
   110	
   111	                <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-3">
   112	                  <Link
   113	                    href="/trip-builder"
   114	                    className="rounded-2xl border border-slate-200 bg-white px-5 py-3 text-sm font-semibold text-slate-800 transition hover:bg-slate-50"
   115	                  >
   116	                    Edit Search
   117	                  </Link>
   118	
   119	                  {selectedPackageId ? (
   120	                    <Link
   121	                      href="/customize"
   122	                      className="rounded-2xl bg-slate-950 px-5 py-3 text-sm font-semibold text-white transition hover:bg-slate-800"
   123	                    >
   124	                      Continue to Customize
   125	                    </Link>
   126	                  ) : null}
   127	                </div>
   128	              </div>
   129	
   130	              <div className="mt-6 flex flex-wrap gap-3">
   131	                {[
   132	                  `Budget: ${budget}`,
   133	                  "Package-led recommendations",
   134	                  "Custom edits available next",
   135	                ].map((item) => (
   136	                  <span
   137	                    key={item}
   138	                    className="rounded-full border border-sky-200 bg-sky-50 px-3 py-1.5 text-xs font-semibold text-sky-700"
   139	                  >
   140	                    {item}
   141	                  </span>
   142	                ))}
   143	              </div>
   144	            </div>
   145	          </div>
   146	        </section>
   147	
   148	        <section className="mx-auto max-w-7xl px-4 py-10 sm:px-6 lg:px-8 lg:py-14">
   149	          <div className="grid gap-8 lg:grid-cols-[300px_1fr]">
   150	            <aside className="space-y-6">
   151	              <div className="rounded-[36px] border border-slate-200 bg-white p-6 shadow-[0_20px_70px_rgba(15,23,42,0.05)]">
   152	                <h2 className="text-lg font-semibold text-slate-950">Trip Filters</h2>
   153	                <div className="mt-5 space-y-4 text-sm">
   154	                  {[
   155	                    `Budget: ${budget}`,
   156	                    `Style: ${travelStyle}`,
   157	                    `Travellers: ${adults + children}`,
   158	                    tripLabel ? `Route: ${tripLabel}` : "Route: Bangkok",
   159	                  ].map((item) => (
   160	                    <div
   161	                      key={item}
   162	                      className="rounded-2xl bg-slate-50 px-4 py-3 text-slate-700"
   163	                    >
   164	                      {item}
   165	                    </div>
   166	                  ))}
   167	                </div>
   168	              </div>
   169	
   170	              <div className="rounded-[36px] border border-slate-200 bg-white p-6 shadow-[0_20px_70px_rgba(15,23,42,0.05)]">
   171	                <p className="text-sm font-medium text-sky-700">Planning Note</p>
   172	                <p className="mt-3 text-sm leading-7 text-slate-600">
   173	                  Select a package to continue. In the next step you can refine room preference,
   174	                  extras, and trip-level choices before review.
   175	                </p>
   176	              </div>
   177	            </aside>
   178	
   179	            <section className="space-y-6">
   180	              {recommendedPackages.map((item) => {
   181	                const isSelected = selectedPackageId === item.id;
   182	
   183	                return (
   184	                  <div
   185	                    key={item.id}
   186	                    className={`overflow-hidden rounded-[36px] border bg-white shadow-[0_20px_70px_rgba(15,23,42,0.06)] transition ${
   187	                      isSelected ? "border-sky-300 ring-2 ring-sky-100" : "border-slate-200"
   188	                    }`}
   189	                  >
   190	                    <div className="grid gap-0 xl:grid-cols-[1.1fr_0.9fr]">
   191	                      <div className="p-6 sm:p-8">
   192	                        <div className="flex flex-wrap items-center gap-3">
   193	                          <span className="inline-flex rounded-full border border-sky-200 bg-sky-50 px-3 py-1 text-xs font-semibold text-sky-700">
   194	                            {item.tag}
   195	                          </span>
   196	                          {isSelected ? (
   197	                            <span className="inline-flex rounded-full border border-emerald-200 bg-emerald-50 px-3 py-1 text-xs font-semibold text-emerald-700">
   198	                              Selected
   199	                            </span>
   200	                          ) : null}
   201	                        </div>
   202	
   203	                        <h2 className="mt-4 text-2xl font-semibold text-slate-950 sm:text-3xl">
   204	                          {item.title}
   205	                        </h2>
   206	
   207	                        <div className="mt-5 grid gap-3 sm:grid-cols-3">
   208	                          <div className="rounded-2xl bg-slate-50 px-4 py-3 text-sm text-slate-700">
   209	                            {item.nights} Nights
   210	                          </div>
   211	                          <div className="rounded-2xl bg-slate-50 px-4 py-3 text-sm text-slate-700">
   212	                            {item.hotelCategory}
   213	                          </div>
   214	                          <div className="rounded-2xl bg-slate-50 px-4 py-3 text-sm text-slate-700">
   215	                            {item.area}
   216	                          </div>
   217	                        </div>
   218	
   219	                        <div className="mt-6 flex flex-wrap gap-3">
   220	                          {item.includes.map((tag) => (
   221	                            <span
   222	                              key={tag}
   223	                              className="rounded-full bg-slate-100 px-3 py-1 text-xs font-medium text-slate-700"

     7	
     8	const extraOptions = [
     9	  "Breakfast included",
    10	  "Indian meal support",
    11	  "SIM card",
    12	  "Travel insurance",
    13	  "Early check-in",
    14	  "Late check-out",
    15	];
    16	
    17	const roomOptions = ["Deluxe Room", "Suite", "Pool View"];
    18	
    19	export default function CustomizePage() {
    20	  const selectedPackageTitle = useTripBuilderStore((state) => state.selectedPackageTitle);
    21	  const selectedPackagePrice = useTripBuilderStore((state) => state.selectedPackagePrice);
    22	  const selectedExtras = useTripBuilderStore((state) => state.selectedExtras);
    23	  const roomPreference = useTripBuilderStore((state) => state.roomPreference);
    24	  const serviceFee = useTripBuilderStore((state) => state.serviceFee);
    25	  const estimatedGrandTotal = useTripBuilderStore((state) => state.estimatedGrandTotal);
    26	  const estimatedTransferTotal = useTripBuilderStore((state) => state.estimatedTransferTotal);
    27	  const estimatedSightseeingTotal = useTripBuilderStore((state) => state.estimatedSightseeingTotal);
    28	  const estimatedMealsTotal = useTripBuilderStore((state) => state.estimatedMealsTotal);
    29	  const toggleExtra = useTripBuilderStore((state) => state.toggleExtra);
    30	  const setRoomPreference = useTripBuilderStore((state) => state.setRoomPreference);
    31	
    32	  const fallbackExtrasTotal = selectedExtras.length * 900;
    33	  const total =
    34	    estimatedGrandTotal > 0
    35	      ? estimatedGrandTotal
    36	      : selectedPackagePrice + fallbackExtrasTotal + serviceFee;
    37	
    38	  return (
    39	    <div className="min-h-screen bg-[linear-gradient(180deg,#f8fbff_0%,#f8fafc_35%,#ffffff_100%)]">
    40	      <PublicHeader />
    41	
    42	      <main>
    43	        <section className="border-b border-slate-200/70 bg-white/60">
    44	          <div className="mx-auto max-w-7xl px-4 py-14 sm:px-6 lg:px-8">
    45	            <div className="max-w-3xl">
    46	              <span className="inline-flex rounded-full border border-sky-200 bg-sky-50 px-3 py-1 text-[11px] font-semibold uppercase tracking-[0.22em] text-sky-700">
    47	                Customize
    48	              </span>
    49	              <h1 className="mt-4 text-4xl font-semibold tracking-tight text-slate-950 sm:text-5xl">
    50	                Personalize your trip before review.
    51	              </h1>
    52	              <p className="mt-4 text-base leading-8 text-slate-600 sm:text-lg">
    53	                Fine-tune room preference and useful extras, then continue to your final review.
    54	              </p>
    55	            </div>
    56	          </div>
    57	        </section>
    58	
    59	        <section className="mx-auto max-w-7xl px-4 py-10 sm:px-6 lg:px-8 lg:py-14">
    60	          <div className="grid gap-8 xl:grid-cols-[1.05fr_0.95fr]">
    61	            <section className="rounded-[36px] border border-slate-200 bg-white p-6 shadow-[0_20px_70px_rgba(15,23,42,0.06)] sm:p-8">
    62	              <div>
    63	                <h2 className="text-2xl font-semibold text-slate-950">
    64	                  {selectedPackageTitle || "Selected trip package"}
    65	                </h2>
    66	                <p className="mt-2 text-sm text-slate-600">
    67	                  Package and trip-level refinements
    68	                </p>
    69	              </div>
    70	
    71	              <div className="mt-8">
    72	                <h3 className="text-base font-semibold text-slate-950">Useful extras</h3>
    73	                <div className="mt-4 grid gap-3 sm:grid-cols-2">
    74	                  {extraOptions.map((item) => {
    75	                    const isActive = selectedExtras.includes(item);
    76	
    77	                    return (
    78	                      <button
    79	                        key={item}
    80	                        type="button"
    81	                        onClick={() => toggleExtra(item)}
    82	                        className={`rounded-[24px] border px-4 py-4 text-left text-sm font-medium transition ${
    83	                          isActive
    84	                            ? "border-sky-200 bg-sky-50 text-sky-700"
    85	                            : "border-slate-200 bg-white text-slate-700 hover:bg-slate-50"
    86	                        }`}
    87	                      >
    88	                        {item}
    89	                      </button>
    90	                    );
    91	                  })}
    92	                </div>
    93	              </div>
    94	
    95	              <div className="mt-8">
    96	                <h3 className="text-base font-semibold text-slate-950">Room Preference</h3>

   100	                      key={item}

   121	                />
   122	              </div>

   135	                  </div>

   138	                    <span className="text-slate-500">Transfers estimate</span>
   139	                    <span className="font-medium text-slate-950">

     2	
     3	import Link from "next/link";

     6	import { PublicFooter } from "@/components/public/public-footer";
     7	import { useTripBuilderStore } from "@/store/useTripBuilderStore";
     8	
     9	export default function ConfirmationPage() {

    11	  const bookingIdFromRoute = String(params.bookingId ?? "");
    12	
    13	  const selectedPackageTitle = useTripBuilderStore((state) => state.selectedPackageTitle);
    14	  const selectedPackagePrice = useTripBuilderStore((state) => state.selectedPackagePrice);
    15	  const adults = useTripBuilderStore((state) => state.adults);

    55	          </p>

    58	            <div className="grid gap-4 sm:grid-cols-2">
    59	              <InfoCard label="Booking ID" value={bookingId || "Pending"} />
    60	              <InfoCard label="Trip" value={selectedPackageTitle || "Selected trip"} />

    77	                      <span
    78	                        key={item}
    79	                        className="rounded-full bg-slate-100 px-3 py-1 text-xs font-medium text-slate-700"
    80	                      >
    81	                        {item}
    82	                      </span>
    83	                    ))
    84	                  ) : (
    85	                    <p className="font-semibold text-slate-950">No extras selected</p>
    86	                  )}
    87	                </div>
    88	              </div>
    89	
    90	              <InfoCard
    91	                label="Package Base"
    92	                value={`₹${selectedPackagePrice.toLocaleString("en-IN")}`}
    93	              />
    94	
    95	              <InfoCard
    96	                label="Hotel Estimate"
    97	                value={`₹${estimatedHotelTotal.toLocaleString("en-IN")}`}
    98	              />
    99	
   100	              <InfoCard
   101	                label="Transfer Estimate"
   102	                value={`₹${estimatedTransferTotal.toLocaleString("en-IN")}`}
   103	              />
   104	
   105	              <InfoCard
   106	                label="Sightseeing Estimate"
   107	                value={`₹${estimatedSightseeingTotal.toLocaleString("en-IN")}`}
   108	              />
   109	
   110	              <InfoCard
   111	                label="Meals / Extras Estimate"
   112	                value={`₹${Math.max(estimatedMealsTotal, fallbackExtrasTotal).toLocaleString("en-IN")}`}
   113	              />
   114	
   115	              <InfoCard
   116	                label="Service Charges"
   117	                value={`₹${serviceFee.toLocaleString("en-IN")}`}
   118	              />
   119	
   120	              <div className="rounded-[24px] bg-white p-5 ring-1 ring-slate-200 sm:col-span-2">
   121	                <p className="text-sm text-slate-500">Final Price</p>
   122	                <p className="mt-2 text-xl font-semibold text-slate-950">
   123	                  ₹{finalPrice.toLocaleString("en-IN")}
   124	                </p>
   125	                <p className="mt-2 text-sm text-slate-500">
   126	                  This reflects the current centralized trip estimate carried forward from your
   127	                  builder, customize, and review flow.
   128	                </p>
   129	              </div>
   130	            </div>
   131	          </div>
   132	
   133	          <div className="mt-10 flex flex-wrap items-center justify-center gap-4">
   134	            <Link
   135	              href="/"
   136	              className="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-2xl bg-slate-950 px-6 py-3.5 text-sm font-semibold text-white transition hover:bg-slate-800"
   137	            >
   138	              Back to Home
   139	            </Link>
   140	
   141	            <Link
   142	              href="/trip-builder"
   143	              className="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-2xl border border-slate-200 bg-white px-6 py-3.5 text-sm font-semibold text-slate-800 transition hover:bg-slate-50"
   144	            >
   145	              Start Another Trip
   146	            </Link>
   147	          </div>
   148	        </div>
   149	      </main>
   150	
   151	      <PublicFooter />
   152	    </div>
   153	  );
   154	}
   155	
   156	function InfoCard({ label, value }: { label: string; value: string }) {
   157	  return (
   158	    <div className="rounded-[24px] bg-white p-5 ring-1 ring-slate-200">
   159	      <p className="text-sm text-slate-500">{label}</p>
   160	      <p className="mt-2 font-semibold text-slate-950">{value}</p>
   161	    </div>
   162	  );
   163	}===== END: src/app/(public)/confirmation/[bookingId]/page.tsx =====

===== START: src/components/public/public-header.tsx =====
     1	"use client";
     2	
     3	import Link from "next/link";
     4	import { useEffect, useRef, useState } from "react";
     5	
     6	const navItems = [
     7	  { label: "Destinations", href: "/results" },
     8	  { label: "Packages", href: "/results" },
     9	  { label: "Plan Your Trip", href: "/trip-builder" },
    10	  { label: "Contact", href: "/" },
    11	];
    12	
    13	export function PublicHeader() {
    14	  const [visible, setVisible] = useState(true);
    15	  const lastY = useRef(0);
    16	
    17	  useEffect(() => {
    18	    const onScroll = () => {
    19	      const currentY = window.scrollY;
    20	
    21	      if (currentY < 20) {
    22	        setVisible(true);
    23	        lastY.current = currentY;
    24	        return;
    25	      }
    26	
    27	      if (currentY > lastY.current && currentY > 80) {
    28	        setVisible(false);
    29	      } else {
    30	        setVisible(true);
    31	      }
    32	
    33	      lastY.current = currentY;
    34	    };
    35	
    36	    window.addEventListener("scroll", onScroll, { passive: true });
    37	    return () => window.removeEventListener("scroll", onScroll);
    38	  }, []);
    39	
    40	  return (
    41	    <header
    42	      className={`fixed inset-x-0 top-3 z-[70] px-3 transition-all duration-300 sm:top-5 sm:px-5 ${
    43	        visible
    44	          ? "translate-y-0 opacity-100"
    45	          : "-translate-y-5 pointer-events-none opacity-0"
    46	      }`}
    47	    >
    48	      <div className="mx-auto max-w-7xl">
    49	        <div className="flex items-center justify-between rounded-[30px] bg-[#f6f1e8]/72 px-4 py-3 backdrop-blur-xl sm:px-6">
    50	          <Link href="/" className="flex items-center gap-3">
    51	            <div className="flex h-10 w-10 items-center justify-center rounded-2xl bg-[linear-gradient(135deg,#0f172a_0%,#f97316_100%)] text-xs font-bold text-white shadow-[0_10px_24px_rgba(15,23,42,0.18)]">
    52	              ET
    53	            </div>
    54	            <div>
    55	              <p className="text-[11px] font-semibold tracking-[0.18em] text-slate-900 sm:text-xs">
    56	                EASYTRIP365
    57	              </p>
    58	              <p className="text-[10px] text-slate-500 sm:text-xs">
    59	                Curated holiday journeys
    60	              </p>
    61	            </div>
    62	          </Link>
    63	
    64	          <nav className="hidden items-center gap-3 lg:flex">
    65	            {navItems.map((item) => (
    66	              <Link
    67	                key={item.label}
    68	                href={item.href}
    69	                className="rounded-full border border-black/70 bg-transparent px-5 py-2.5 text-sm font-medium text-slate-800 transition hover:border-black hover:text-slate-950"
    70	              >
    71	                {item.label}
    72	              </Link>
    73	            ))}
    74	          </nav>
    75	
    76	          <Link
    77	            href="/trip-builder"
    78	            className="inline-flex rounded-full bg-orange-500 px-5 py-2.5 text-sm font-semibold text-white shadow-[0_14px_30px_rgba(249,115,22,0.28)] transition hover:bg-orange-600"
    79	          >
    80	            Start Planning
    81	          </Link>
    82	        </div>
    83	      </div>
    84	    </header>
    85	  );
    86	}

   259	export const useTripBuilderStore = create<TripBuilderState>((set) => ({
   260	  ...initialState,
   261	
   262	  setTripDetails: (payload) =>
   263	    set((state) => ({
   264	      ...state,
   265	      ...payload,
   266	    })),
   267	
   268	  setSelectedMode: (mode) =>
   269	    set(() => ({
   270	      selectedMode: mode,
   271	    })),
   272	
   273	  setBudget: (value) =>
   274	    set(() => ({
   275	      budget: value,
   276	    })),
   277	
   278	  setMood: (value) =>
   279	    set(() => ({
   280	      mood: value,
   281	    })),
   282	
   283	  setTravelStyle: (value) =>
   284	    set(() => ({
   285	      travelStyle: value,
   286	    })),
   287	
   288	  setTravellingWith: (value) =>
   289	    set(() => ({
   290	      travellingWith: value,
   291	    })),
   292	
   293	  setPriority: (value) =>
   294	    set(() => ({
   295	      priority: value,
   296	    })),
   297	
   298	  setSpecialRequest: (value) =>
   299	    set(() => ({
   300	      specialRequest: value,
   301	    })),
   302	
   303	  setSegments: (segments) =>
   304	    set(() => ({
   305	      segments,
   306	    })),
   307	
   308	  addSegment: () =>
   309	    set((state) => ({
   310	      segments: [
   311	        ...state.segments,
   312	        {
   313	          id: `segment-${Date.now()}`,
   314	          city: "",
   315	          destinationId: "",
   316	          checkIn: "",
   317	          checkOut: "",
   318	        },
   319	      ],
   320	    })),
   321	
   322	  updateSegment: (id, values) =>
   323	    set((state) => ({
   324	      segments: state.segments.map((segment) => {
   325	        if (segment.id !== id) return segment;
   326	
   327	        const next = { ...segment, ...values };
   328	
   329	        if (
   330	          next.checkIn &&
   331	          next.checkOut &&
   332	          new Date(next.checkOut).getTime() <= new Date(next.checkIn).getTime()
   333	        ) {
   334	          next.checkOut = "";
   335	        }
   336	
   337	        return next;
   338	      }),
   339	    })),
   340	
   341	  removeSegment: (id) =>
   342	    set((state) => ({
   343	      segments:
   344	        state.segments.length <= 1
   345	          ? state.segments
   346	          : state.segments.filter((segment) => segment.id !== id),
   347	    })),
   348	
   349	  setArrivalTimeSlot: (value) =>
   350	    set(() => ({
   351	      arrivalTimeSlot: value,
   352	    })),
   353	
   354	  setDepartureTimeSlot: (value) =>
   355	    set(() => ({
   356	      departureTimeSlot: value,
   357	    })),
   358	
   359	  setTravelers: ({ adults, children, rooms }) =>
   360	    set((state) => ({
   361	      adults: adults ?? state.adults,
   362	      children: children ?? state.children,
   363	      rooms: rooms ?? state.rooms,
   364	    })),
   365	
   366	  togglePreference: (value) =>
   367	    set((state) => ({
   368	      specialPreferences: state.specialPreferences.includes(value)
   369	        ? state.specialPreferences.filter((item) => item !== value)
   370	        : [...state.specialPreferences, value],
   371	    })),
   372	
   373	  setAiPrompt: (value) =>
   374	    set(() => ({
   375	      aiPrompt: value,
   376	    })),
   377	
   378	  addAiChatMessage: (message) =>
   379	    set((state) => ({
   380	      aiChatMessages: [...state.aiChatMessages, message],
   381	    })),
   382	
   383	  resetAiChat: () =>
   384	    set(() => ({
   385	      aiChatMessages: initialAiMessages,
   386	    })),
   387	
   388	  selectPackage: ({ selectedPackageId, selectedPackageTitle, selectedPackagePrice }) =>
   389	    set(() => ({
   390	      selectedPackageId,
   391	      selectedPackageTitle,
   392	      selectedPackagePrice,
   393	    })),
   394	
   395	  setSelectedHotelId: (value) =>
   396	    set(() => ({
   397	      selectedHotelId: value,
   398	    })),
   399	
   400	  setHotelCategory: (value) =>
   401	    set(() => ({
   402	      hotelCategory: value,
   403	    })),
   404	
   405	  setSelectedArrivalTransferId: (value) =>
   406	    set(() => ({
   407	      selectedArrivalTransferId: value,
   408	    })),
   409	
   410	  setSelectedDepartureTransferId: (value) =>
   411	    set(() => ({
   412	      selectedDepartureTransferId: value,
   413	    })),
   414	
   415	  setSelectedLocalTransferId: (value) =>
   416	    set(() => ({

   419

   470	      estimatedGrandTotal: payload.estimatedGrandTotal ?? state.estimatedGrandTotal,
   471	    })),

===== START: src/lib/helpers/pricing.ts =====
     1	import { transfers, type Transfer, type TransferPurpose } from "@/data/transfers";
     2	import type { Hotel } from "@/data/hotels";
     3	
     4	export type PricedItem = {
     5	  id: string;
     6	  price?: number;
     7	  quantity?: number;
     8	};
     9	
    10	export type PassengerMix = {
    11	  adults: number;
    12	  children: number;
    13	};
    14	
    15	export function getTotalPassengers({ adults, children }: PassengerMix): number {
    16	  return Math.max(0, adults) + Math.max(0, children);
    17	}
    18	
    19	export function calculateNights(checkIn?: string, checkOut?: string): number {
    20	  if (!checkIn || !checkOut) return 0;
    21	
    22	  const start = new Date(checkIn);
    23	  const end = new Date(checkOut);
    24	
    25	  if (Number.isNaN(start.getTime()) || Number.isNaN(end.getTime())) return 0;
    26	
    27	  const diffMs = end.getTime() - start.getTime();
    28	  const nights = Math.floor(diffMs / (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24));
    29	
    30	  return nights > 0 ? nights : 0;
    31	}
    32	
    33	export function getRecommendedTransfer(params: {
    34	  adults: number;
    35	  children: number;
    36	  purpose: TransferPurpose;
    37	  destinationId?: string;
    38	  preferPremium?: boolean;
    39	}): Transfer | null {
    40	  const totalPax = getTotalPassengers({
    41	    adults: params.adults,
    42	    children: params.children,
    43	  });
    44	
    45	  const destinationId = params.destinationId ?? "dest-bangkok";
    46	
    47	  const matching = transfers.filter(
    48	    (item) =>
    49	      item.isActive &&
    50	      item.purpose === params.purpose &&
    51	      item.destinationIds.includes(destinationId) &&
    52	      totalPax >= item.minPax &&
    53	      totalPax <= item.maxPax
    54	  );
    55	
    56	  if (!matching.length) return null;
    57	
    58	  if (params.preferPremium) {
    59	    const premium = matching.find((item) => item.serviceType === "premium-private");
    60	    if (premium) return premium;
    61	  }
    62	
    63	  const preferredOrder = ["private", "premium-private", "shared"];
    64	
    65	  const sorted = [...matching].sort((a, b) => {
    66	    const serviceScore =
    67	      preferredOrder.indexOf(a.serviceType) - preferredOrder.indexOf(b.serviceType);
    68	
    69	    if (serviceScore !== 0) return serviceScore;
    70	
    71	    const vehicleOrder = ["sedan", "suv", "van", "mini-coach", "seat-in-coach"];
    72	    return vehicleOrder.indexOf(a.vehicleClass) - vehicleOrder.indexOf(b.vehicleClass);
    73	  });
    74	
    75	  return sorted[0] ?? null;
    76	}
    77	
    78	export function calculateHotelTotal(params: {
    79	  hotel: Hotel | null;
    80	  nights: number;
    81	  rooms: number;
    82	}): number {
    83	  if (!params.hotel || params.nights <= 0 || params.rooms <= 0) return 0;
    84	
    85	  return params.hotel.nightlyRate * params.nights * params.rooms;
    86	}
    87	
    88	export function calculateHotelMargin(params: {
    89	  hotel: Hotel | null;
    90	  nights: number;
    91	  rooms: number;
    92	}): number {
    93	  if (!params.hotel || params.nights <= 0 || params.rooms <= 0) return 0;
    94	
    95	  return params.hotel.margin * params.nights * params.rooms;
    96	}
    97	
    98	export function calculateSightseeingTotal(
    99	  selectedItems: Array<PricedItem>,
   100	  passengerCount = 1
   101	): number {
   102	  return selectedItems.reduce((sum, item) => {
   103	    const quantity = item.quantity ?? passengerCount;
   104	    return sum + (item.price ?? 0) * quantity;
   105	  }, 0);
   106	}
   107	
   108	export function calculateMealsTotal(
   109	  selectedItems: Array<PricedItem>,
   110	  passengerCount = 1
   111	): number {
   112	  return selectedItems.reduce((sum, item) => {
   113	    const quantity = item.quantity ?? passengerCount;
   114	    return sum + (item.price ?? 0) * quantity;
   115	  }, 0);
   116	}
   117	
   118	export function calculateTransferTotal(params: {
   119	  arrivalTransfer?: Transfer | null;
   120	  departureTransfer?: Transfer | null;
   121	  localTransfer?: Transfer | null;
   122	}): number {
   123	  return (
   124	    (params.arrivalTransfer?.price ?? 0) +
   125	    (params.departureTransfer?.price ?? 0) +
   126	    (params.localTransfer?.price ?? 0)
   127	  );
   128	}
   129	
   130	export function calculateTransferMargin(params: {
   131	  arrivalTransfer?: Transfer | null;
   132	  departureTransfer?: Transfer | null;
   133	  localTransfer?: Transfer | null;
   134	}): number {
   135	  return (
   136	    (params.arrivalTransfer?.margin ?? 0) +
   137	    (params.departureTransfer?.margin ?? 0) +
   138	    (params.localTransfer?.margin ?? 0)
   139	  );
   140	}
   141	
   142	export function calculateBasePackagePrice(basePrice: number): number {
   143	  return basePrice > 0 ? basePrice : 0;
   144	}
   145	
   146	export function calculateHotelDelta(delta: number): number {
   147	  return delta > 0 ? delta : 0;
   148	}
   149	
   150	export function calculateGrandTotal(params: {
   151	  basePrice?: number;
   152	  hotelTotal?: number;
   153	  hotelDelta?: number;
   154	  transferTotal?: number;
   155	  sightseeingTotal?: number;
   156	  mealsTotal?: number;
   157	  serviceFee?: number;
   158	}): number {
   159	  return (
   160	    (params.basePrice ?? 0) +
   161	    (params.hotelTotal ?? 0) +
   162	    (params.hotelDelta ?? 0) +
   163	    (params.transferTotal ?? 0) +
   164	    (params.sightseeingTotal ?? 0) +
   165	    (params.mealsTotal ?? 0) +
   166	    (params.serviceFee ?? 0)
   167	  );
   168	}
   169	
   170	export function calculateTripGrandTotal(params: {
   171	  packageBasePrice?: number;
   172	  hotel: Hotel | null;
   173	  nights: number;
   174	  rooms: number;
   175	  arrivalTransfer?: Transfer | null;
   176	  departureTransfer?: Transfer | null;
   177	  localTransfer?: Transfer | null;
   178	  sightseeingItems?: Array<PricedItem>;
   179	  mealItems?: Array<PricedItem>;
   180	  passengerCount: number;
   181	  serviceFee?: number;
   182	  includeStandaloneHotel?: boolean;
   183	}): number {
   184	  const hotelTotal = params.includeStandaloneHotel
   185	    ? calculateHotelTotal({
   186	        hotel: params.hotel,
   187	        nights: params.nights,
   188	        rooms: params.rooms,
   189	      })
   190	    : 0;
   191	
   192	  const transferTotal = calculateTransferTotal({
   193	    arrivalTransfer: params.arrivalTransfer,
   194	    departureTransfer: params.departureTransfer,
   195	    localTransfer: params.localTransfer,
   196	  });
   197	
   198	  const sightseeingTotal = calculateSightseeingTotal(
   199	    params.sightseeingItems ?? [],
   200	    params.passengerCount
   201	  );
   202	
   203	  const mealsTotal = calculateMealsTotal(params.mealItems ?? [], params.passengerCount);
   204	
   205	  return calculateGrandTotal({
   206	    basePrice: params.packageBasePrice ?? 0,
   207	    hotelTotal,
   208	    transferTotal,
   209	    sightseeingTotal,
   210	    mealsTotal,
   211	    serviceFee: params.serviceFee ?? 0,
   212	  });
   213	}===== END: src/lib/helpers/pricing.ts =====

===== START: src/lib/helpers/recommendation.ts =====
     1	import type { Hotel, HotelTag } from "@/data/hotels";
     2	import { hotels } from "@/data/hotels";
     3	import {
     4	  getRecommendedTransfer as getRecommendedTransferFromPricing,
     5	} from "@/lib/helpers/pricing";

     8	export type PackageLike = {
     9	  id: string;
    10	  title: string;
    11	  basePrice: number;
    12	  popularityScore?: number;
    13	  marginScore?: number;
    14	  budgetFitScore?: number;
    15	  tripMoodFitScore?: number;
    16	  recommendedLabel?: string;
    17	};
    18	
    19	export type TripDayType =
    20	  | "arrival"
    21	  | "full-day"
    22	  | "relaxed"
    23	  | "departure";
    24	
    25	export type DayPlan = {
    26	  dayNumber: number;
    27	  label: string;
    28	  dayType: TripDayType;
    29	  allowedTimeSlots: Array<"morning" | "afternoon" | "evening" | "night">;
    30	  notes: string[];
    31	};
    32	
    33	type BuildTripDayParams = {
    34	  nights: number;
    35	  arrivalTimeSlot?: "early-morning" | "morning" | "afternoon" | "evening" | "night";
    36	  departureTimeSlot?: "morning" | "afternoon" | "evening" | "night";
    37	};
    38	
    39	export function getRecommendedPackages(packages: PackageLike[]): PackageLike[] {
    40	  return [...packages]
    41	    .sort((a, b) => {
    42	      const scoreA =
    43	        (a.popularityScore || 0) +
    44	        (a.marginScore || 0) +
    45	        (a.budgetFitScore || 0) +
    46	        (a.tripMoodFitScore || 0);
    47	
    48	      const scoreB =
    49	        (b.popularityScore || 0) +
    50	        (b.marginScore || 0) +
    51	        (b.budgetFitScore || 0) +
    52	        (b.tripMoodFitScore || 0);
    53	
    54	      return scoreB - scoreA;
    55	    })
    56	    .slice(0, 6);
    57	}
    58	
    59	export function getPackageBadge(pkg: PackageLike): string {
    60	  if (pkg.recommendedLabel) return pkg.recommendedLabel;
    61	  if ((pkg.popularityScore || 0) >= 9) return "Most Booked";
    62	  if ((pkg.budgetFitScore || 0) >= 9) return "Best Value";
    63	  if ((pkg.tripMoodFitScore || 0) >= 9) return "Great Match for You";
    64	  if ((pkg.marginScore || 0) >= 9) return "Top Pick";
    65	  return "Popular Choice";
    66	}
    67	
    68	export function getRecommendationReason(pkg: PackageLike): string {
    69	  if ((pkg.tripMoodFitScore || 0) >= 9) {
    70	    return "This package strongly matches your selected trip mood.";
    71	  }
    72	
    73	  if ((pkg.budgetFitScore || 0) >= 9) {
    74	    return "This package gives a strong balance of experience and value.";
    75	  }
    76	
    77	  if ((pkg.popularityScore || 0) >= 9) {
    78	    return "Travelers choose this package often for its overall convenience.";
    79	  }
    80	
    81	  if ((pkg.marginScore || 0) >= 9) {
    82	    return "This option includes premium value additions and smoother experience.";
    83	  }
    84	
    85	  return "This is a solid all-round option for your travel plan.";
    86	}
    87	
    88	export function buildTripDayPlans(params: BuildTripDayParams): DayPlan[] {
    89	  const totalDays = Math.max(1, params.nights + 1);
    90	  const plans: DayPlan[] = [];
    91	
    92	  for (let day = 1; day <= totalDays; day += 1) {
    93	    if (day === 1) {
    94	      const notes = ["Arrival day should stay light and practical."];
    95	
    96	      if (
    97	        params.arrivalTimeSlot === "early-morning" ||
    98	        params.arrivalTimeSlot === "morning"
    99	      ) {
   100	        notes.push("Avoid strict early-entry sightseeing after overnight flights.");
   101	        plans.push({
   102	          dayNumber: day,
   103	          label: "Arrival Day",
   104	          dayType: "arrival",
   105	          allowedTimeSlots: ["afternoon", "evening", "night"],
   106	          notes,
   107	        });
   108	      } else {
   109	        notes.push("Keep the plan flexible around check-in and rest.");
   110	        plans.push({
   111	          dayNumber: day,
   112	          label: "Arrival Day",
   113	          dayType: "arrival",
   114	          allowedTimeSlots: ["evening", "night"],
   115	          notes,
   116	        });
   117	      }
   118	
   119	      continue;
   120	    }
   121	
   122	    if (day === totalDays) {
   123	      const notes = ["Departure day should stay operationally safe and buffer-friendly."];
   124	
   125	      if (params.departureTimeSlot === "morning") {
   126	        notes.push("Do not recommend major sightseeing.");
   127	        plans.push({
   128	          dayNumber: day,
   129	          label: "Departure Day",
   130	          dayType: "departure",
   131	          allowedTimeSlots: [],
   132	          notes,
   133	        });
   134	      } else if (params.departureTimeSlot === "afternoon") {
   135	        notes.push("Only short and nearby activities should be shown.");
   136	        plans.push({
   137	          dayNumber: day,
   138	          label: "Departure Day",
   139	          dayType: "departure",
   140	          allowedTimeSlots: ["morning"],
   141	          notes,
   142	        });
   143	      } else {
   144	        notes.push("A light half-day plan may be possible before airport transfer.");
   145	        plans.push({
   146	          dayNumber: day,
   147	          label: "Departure Day",
   148	          dayType: "departure",
   149	          allowedTimeSlots: ["morning", "afternoon"],
   150	          notes,
   151	        });
   152	      }
   153	
   154	      continue;
   155	    }
   156	
   157	    plans.push({
   158	      dayNumber: day,
   159	      label: `Day ${day}`,
   160	      dayType: "full-day",
   161	      allowedTimeSlots: ["morning", "afternoon", "evening"],
   162	      notes: ["Best suited for primary sightseeing and main city experiences."],
   163	    });
   164	  }
   165	
   166	  return plans;
   167	}
   168	
   169	export function isEarlyStartRestrictedOnArrival(
   170	  arrivalTimeSlot?: "early-morning" | "morning" | "afternoon" | "evening" | "night"
   171	): boolean {
   172	  return arrivalTimeSlot === "early-morning" || arrivalTimeSlot === "morning";
   173	}
   174	
   175	export function getHotelTagMatches(tripStyle: string, travellingWith: string): HotelTag[] {
   176	  const normalizedStyle = tripStyle.toLowerCase();
   177	  const normalizedGroup = travellingWith.toLowerCase();
   178	
   179	  const tags = new Set<HotelTag>();
   180	
   181	  if (normalizedStyle.includes("lux")) tags.add("luxury");
   182	  if (normalizedStyle.includes("shop")) tags.add("shopping");
   183	  if (normalizedStyle.includes("night")) tags.add("nightlife");
   184	  if (normalizedStyle.includes("mixed")) tags.add("first-timer");
   185	  if (normalizedStyle.includes("comfort")) tags.add("premium-comfort");
   186	
   187	  if (normalizedGroup.includes("couple")) tags.add("couple");
   188	  if (normalizedGroup.includes("family")) tags.add("family");
   189	  if (normalizedGroup.includes("friend")) tags.add("nightlife");
   190	
   191	  if (tags.size === 0) {
   192	    tags.add("first-timer");
   193	    tags.add("value");
   194	  }
   195	
   196	  return [...tags];
   197	}
   198	
   199	export function getRecommendedHotels(params: {
   200	  destinationId?: string;
   201	  budget?: string;
   202	  category?: "3 Star" | "4 Star" | "5 Star";
   203	  tripStyle?: string;
   204	  travellingWith?: string;
   205	  limit?: number;
   206	}): Hotel[] {
   207	  const destinationId = params.destinationId ?? "dest-bangkok";
   208	  const requestedTags = getHotelTagMatches(
   209	    params.tripStyle ?? "Mixed",
   210	    params.travellingWith ?? "Couple"
   211	  );
   212	
   213	  return hotels
   214	    .filter(
   215	      (hotel) =>
   216	        hotel.isActive &&
   217	        hotel.destinationId === destinationId &&
   218	        (!params.category || hotel.category === params.category)
   219	    )
   220	    .map((hotel) => {
   221	      const tagScore = hotel.tags.reduce(
   222	        (sum, tag) => sum + (requestedTags.includes(tag) ? 2 : 0),
   223	        0
   224	      );
   225	
   226	      const budgetScore =
   227	        params.budget === "Economy" && hotel.category === "3 Star"
   228	          ? 3
   229	          : params.budget === "Comfort" && hotel.category === "4 Star"
   230	          ? 3
   231	          : (params.budget === "Premium" || params.budget === "Luxury") &&
   232	            hotel.category === "5 Star"
   233	          ? 3
   234	          : 0;
   235	
   236	      const score = tagScore + budgetScore + hotel.rating;
   237	
   238	      return { hotel, score };
   239	    })
   240	    .sort((a, b) => b.score - a.score)
   241	    .slice(0, params.limit ?? 6)
   242	    .map((item) => item.hotel);
   243	}
   244	
   245	export function getRecommendedTransfer(params: {
   246	  adults: number;
   247	  children: number;
   248	  purpose: TransferPurpose;
   249	  destinationId?: string;
   250	  budget?: string;
   251	  travellingWith?: string;
   252	}): Transfer | null {
   253	  const preferPremium =
   254	    params.budget === "Luxury" ||
   255	    params.budget === "Premium" ||
   256	    (params.travellingWith ?? "").toLowerCase().includes("couple");
   257	
   258	  return getRecommendedTransferFromPricing({
   259	    adults: params.adults,
   260	    children: params.children,
   261	    purpose: params.purpose,
   262	    destinationId: params.destinationId ?? "dest-bangkok",
   263	    preferPremium,
   264	  });
   265	}===== END: src/lib/helpers/recommendation.ts =====

     3	type AIGuidedFlowProps = {

    12	  return (value ?? fallback).toLowerCase();

    15	function getRecommendation(params: {
    16	  tripStyle?: string;
    17	  travellingWith?: string;
    18	  budget?: string;
    19	  priority?: string;
    20	  specialRequest?: string;
    21	}) {
    22	  const style = normalize(params.tripStyle, "mixed");
    23	  const group = normalize(params.travellingWith, "couple");
    24	  const budget = normalize(params.budget, "comfort");
    25	  const priority = normalize(params.priority, "value");
    26	  const specialRequest = params.specialRequest?.trim() ?? "";
    27	
    28	  let title = "Balanced Thailand Plan";
    29	  let summary =
    30	    "A well-paced Thailand itinerary with a practical mix of comfort, sightseeing, and free time.";
    31	  let hotelTier = "4★ hotel";
    32	  let route = "Bangkok + Pattaya";
    33	  let nights = "5N / 6D";
    34	
    35	  if (style.includes("luxury")) {
    36	    title = "Luxury Thailand Escape";
    37	    summary =
    38	      "Premium stay selection with smoother transfers, elevated hotel comfort, and slower pacing.";
    39	    hotelTier = "4★ premium stay";
    40	    route = "Bangkok + Pattaya";
    41	    nights = "5N / 6D";
    42	  } else if (style.includes("shopping")) {
    43	    title = "Bangkok Shopping Break";
    44	    summary =
    45	      "Built around city convenience, shopping zones, easy transfers, and flexible evenings.";
    46	    hotelTier = "4★ city hotel";
    47	    route = "Bangkok";
    48	    nights = "4N / 5D";
    49	  } else if (style.includes("nightlife")) {
    50	    title = "Bangkok After Dark";
    51	    summary =
    52	      "A city-led plan with late evenings, central stays, and flexible daytime recovery windows.";
    53	    hotelTier = "4★ central stay";
    54	    route = "Bangkok + Pattaya";
    55	    nights = "4N / 5D";
    56	  } else if (style.includes("family")) {
    57	    title = "Family Fun Thailand";
    58	    summary =
    59	      "A smoother itinerary with practical transfers, family-friendly pacing, and lighter day loads.";
    60	    hotelTier = "4★ family-friendly hotel";
    61	    route = "Bangkok + Pattaya";
    62	    nights = "5N / 6D";
    63	  } else if (style.includes("adventure")) {
    64	    title = "Adventure Thailand Route";
    65	    summary =
    66	      "An active trip structure with day outings, efficient transfers, and tighter routing.";
    67	    hotelTier = "4★ hotel";
    68	    route = "Bangkok + Pattaya";
    69	    nights = "5N / 6D";
    70	  }
    71	
    72	  if (budget.includes("economy")) {
    73	    hotelTier = "3★ hotel";
    74	  } else if (budget.includes("premium") || budget.includes("luxury")) {
    75	    hotelTier = hotelTier.includes("premium") ? hotelTier : "4★ premium stay";
    76	  }
    77	
    78	  const notes: string[] = [];
    79	
    80	  if (group.includes("family")) {
    81	    notes.push("family-friendly pacing");
    82	  }
    83	  if (group.includes("friends")) {
    84	    notes.push("group-friendly rooming and transfers");
    85	  }
    86	  if (group.includes("solo")) {
    87	    notes.push("safer central routing");
    88	  }
    89	  if (priority.includes("value")) {
    90	    notes.push("better value balance");
    91	  }
    92	  if (priority.includes("comfort")) {
    93	    notes.push("higher comfort focus");
    94	  }
    95	  if (priority.includes("fast")) {
    96	    notes.push("faster decision-making");
    97	  }
    98	  if (specialRequest) {
    99	    notes.push(`special request noted: ${specialRequest}`);
   100	  }
   101	
   102	  return {
   103	    title,
   104	    summary,
   105	    hotelTier,
   106	    route,
   107	    nights,
   108	    notes,
   109	  };

   112	export function AIGuidedFlow({
   113	  tripStyle = "mixed",
   114	  travellingWith = "couple",
   115	  budget = "comfort",
   116	  priority = "value",
   117	  specialRequest = "",

   166	          </p>

   184	              balanced recommendation
   185	            </span>
   186	          )}

   189	    </div>

===== START: src/components/trip-builder/bangkok-area-selector.tsx =====
     1	"use client";
     2	
     3	import { useMemo, useState } from "react";
     4	import { bangkokAreas } from "@/lib/mock/bangkok-builder-data";
     5	import { MapPin, Search } from "lucide-react";
     6	
     7	type Props = {
     8	  value: string;
     9	  onChange: (value: string) => void;
    10	};
    11	
    12	export function BangkokAreaSelector({ value, onChange }: Props) {
    13	  const [query, setQuery] = useState("");
    14	
    15	  const filteredAreas = useMemo(() => {
    16	    const base = bangkokAreas.filter((area) =>
    17	      area.name.toLowerCase().includes(query.toLowerCase())
    18	    );
    19	
    20	    if (query.trim()) return base;
    21	
    22	    const popular = bangkokAreas.filter((area) => area.popular);
    23	    const others = bangkokAreas.filter((area) => !area.popular);
    24	    return [...popular, ...others];
    25	  }, [query]);
    26	
    27	  return (
    28	    <div className="rounded-[28px] border border-slate-200 bg-white p-4 shadow-sm">
    29	      <div className="mb-4 flex items-center gap-2">
    30	        <MapPin className="h-5 w-5 text-sky-600" />
    31	        <div>
    32	          <p className="text-sm font-semibold text-slate-950">
    33	            Where do you want to stay?
    34	          </p>
    35	          <p className="text-xs text-slate-500">
    36	            Choose the city or stay area that should shape better hotel suggestions
    37	          </p>
    38	        </div>
    39	      </div>
    40	
    41	      <div className="relative mb-4">
    42	        <Search className="pointer-events-none absolute left-4 top-1/2 h-4 w-4 -translate-y-1/2 text-slate-400" />
    43	        <input
    44	          type="text"
    45	          placeholder="Search city or area"
    46	          value={query}
    47	          onChange={(e) => setQuery(e.target.value)}
    48	          className="w-full rounded-2xl border border-slate-200 bg-slate-50 py-3 pl-11 pr-4 text-sm text-slate-950 outline-none transition focus:border-sky-400 focus:bg-white"
    49	        />
    50	      </div>
    51	
    52	      <div className="grid gap-3 md:grid-cols-2 xl:grid-cols-3">
    53	        {filteredAreas.map((area) => {
    54	          const active = value === area.name;
    55	
    56	          return (
    57	            <button
    58	              key={area.id}
    59	              type="button"
    60	              onClick={() => onChange(area.name)}
    61	              className={`rounded-2xl border p-4 text-left transition ${
    62	                active
    63	                  ? "border-sky-500 bg-sky-50"
    64	                  : "border-slate-200 bg-slate-50 hover:border-slate-300 hover:bg-white"
    65	              }`}
    66	            >
    67	              <div className="flex items-center justify-between gap-3">
    68	                <span className="text-sm font-semibold text-slate-950">{area.name}</span>
    69	                {area.popular ? (
    70	                  <span className="rounded-full bg-slate-900 px-2.5 py-1 text-[11px] font-medium text-white">
    71	                    Popular
    72	                  </span>
    73	                ) : null}
    74	              </div>
    75	              <p className="mt-2 text-xs leading-5 text-slate-600">{area.shortDescription}</p>
    76	            </button>
    77	          );
    78	        })}
    79	      </div>

===== START: src/components/trip-builder/city-route-planner.tsx =====
     1	"use client";
     2	
     3	import { useMemo } from "react";
     4	import { MapPin, Plus, Trash2 } from "lucide-react";
     5	import { thailandCities } from "@/lib/mock/bangkok-builder-data";
     6	
     7	export type TripSegment = {
     8	  id: string;
     9	  city: string;
    10	  destinationId?: string;
    11	  checkIn: string;
    12	  checkOut: string;
    13	};
    14	
    15	type Props = {
    16	  segments: TripSegment[];
    17	  onAddSegment: () => void;
    18	  onRemoveSegment: (id: string) => void;
    19	  onUpdateSegment: (
    20	    id: string,
    21	    values: Partial<{
    22	      city: string;
    23	      destinationId?: string;
    24	      checkIn: string;
    25	      checkOut: string;
    26	    }>
    27	  ) => void;
    28	};
    29	
    30	function getNights(checkIn: string, checkOut: string) {
    31	  if (!checkIn || !checkOut) return 0;
    32	
    33	  const start = new Date(checkIn);
    34	  const end = new Date(checkOut);
    35	
    36	  if (Number.isNaN(start.getTime()) || Number.isNaN(end.getTime())) return 0;
    37	
    38	  const diff = Math.floor((end.getTime() - start.getTime()) / (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24));
    39	  return diff > 0 ? diff : 0;
    40	}
    41	
    42	export function CityRoutePlanner({
    43	  segments,
    44	  onAddSegment,
    45	  onRemoveSegment,
    46	  onUpdateSegment,
    47	}: Props) {
    48	  const totalNights = useMemo(
    49	    () => segments.reduce((sum, item) => sum + getNights(item.checkIn, item.checkOut), 0),
    50	    [segments]
    51	  );
    52	
    53	  return (
    54	    <section className="rounded-[32px] border border-slate-200 bg-white p-5 shadow-sm sm:p-6">
    55	      <div className="flex flex-col gap-4 sm:flex-row sm:items-center sm:justify-between">
    56	        <div>
    57	          <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
    58	            <MapPin className="h-5 w-5 text-sky-600" />
    59	            <h2 className="text-lg font-semibold tracking-tight text-slate-950">
    60	              Route planner
    61	            </h2>
    62	          </div>
    63	          <p className="mt-1 text-sm text-slate-600">
    64	            Add one or multiple city stays. Each stop can have its own dates and nights.
    65	          </p>
    66	        </div>
    67	
    68	        <button
    69	          type="button"
    70	          onClick={onAddSegment}
    71	          className="inline-flex items-center justify-center gap-2 rounded-2xl bg-slate-950 px-4 py-3 text-sm font-semibold text-white transition hover:bg-slate-800"
    72	        >
    73	          <Plus className="h-4 w-4" />
    74	          Add city stay
    75	        </button>
    76	      </div>
    77	
    78	      <div className="mt-6 grid gap-4">
    79	        {segments.map((segment, index) => {
    80	          const nights = getNights(segment.checkIn, segment.checkOut);
    81	
    82	          return (
    83	            <div
    84	              key={segment.id}
    85	              className="rounded-[24px] border border-slate-200 bg-slate-50 p-4"
    86	            >
    87	              <div className="mb-4 flex items-center justify-between gap-3">
    88	                <div>
    89	                  <p className="text-sm font-semibold text-slate-950">
    90	                    Stay {index + 1}
    91	                  </p>
    92	                  <p className="text-xs text-slate-500">
    93	                    {nights > 0 ? `${nights} nights selected` : "Select city and dates"}
    94	                  </p>
    95	                </div>
    96	
    97	                {segments.length > 1 ? (
    98	                  <button
    99	                    type="button"
   100	                    onClick={() => onRemoveSegment(segment.id)}
   101	                    className="inline-flex h-10 w-10 items-center justify-center rounded-xl border border-slate-200 bg-white text-slate-600 transition hover:bg-slate-100"
   102	                  >
   103	                    <Trash2 className="h-4 w-4" />
   104	                  </button>
   105	                ) : null}
   106	              </div>
   107	
   108	              <div className="grid gap-4 lg:grid-cols-[1.1fr_0.9fr_0.9fr_0.5fr]">
   109	                <label className="block">
   110	                  <span className="mb-2 block text-sm font-medium text-slate-700">City</span>
   111	                  <select
   112	                    value={segment.city}
   113	                    onChange={(e) => {
   114	                      const selectedCity = thailandCities.find(
   115	                        (city) => city.name === e.target.value
   116	                      );
   117	
   118	                      onUpdateSegment(segment.id, {
   119	                        city: e.target.value,
   120	                        destinationId: selectedCity?.destinationId ?? "",
   121	                      });
   122	                    }}
   123	                    className="w-full rounded-2xl border border-slate-200 bg-white px-4 py-3 text-sm text-slate-950 outline-none transition focus:border-sky-400"
   124	                  >
   125	                    <option value="">Select city</option>
   126	                    {thailandCities.map((city) => (
   127	                      <option key={city.id} value={city.name}>
   128	                        {city.name} — {city.region}
   129	                      </option>
   130	                    ))}
   131	                  </select>
   132	                </label>
   133	
   134	                <label className="block">
   135	                  <span className="mb-2 block text-sm font-medium text-slate-700">Check-in</span>
   136	                  <input
   137	                    type="date"
   138	                    value={segment.checkIn}
   139	                    onChange={(e) => onUpdateSegment(segment.id, { checkIn: e.target.value })}
   140	                    className="w-full rounded-2xl border border-slate-200 bg-white px-4 py-3 text-sm text-slate-950 outline-none transition focus:border-sky-400"
   141	                  />
   142	                </label>
   143	
   144	                <label className="block">
   145	                  <span className="mb-2 block text-sm font-medium text-slate-700">Check-out</span>
   146	                  <input
   147	                    type="date"
   148	                    min={segment.checkIn || undefined}
   149	                    value={segment.checkOut}
   150	                    onChange={(e) => onUpdateSegment(segment.id, { checkOut: e.target.value })}
   151	                    className="w-full rounded-2xl border border-slate-200 bg-white px-4 py-3 text-sm text-slate-950 outline-none transition focus:border-sky-400"
   152	                  />
   153	                </label>
   154	
   155	                <div className="block">
   156	                  <span className="mb-2 block text-sm font-medium text-slate-700">Nights</span>
   157	                  <div className="flex h-[50px] items-center rounded-2xl border border-slate-200 bg-white px-4 text-sm font-semibold text-slate-950">
   158	                    {nights || 0}
   159	                  </div>
   160	                </div>
   161	              </div>
   162	            </div>
   163	          );
   164	        })}
   165	      </div>
   166	
   167	      <div className="mt-5 rounded-2xl bg-sky-50 px-4 py-3">
   168	        <p className="text-sm font-medium text-slate-900">
   169	          Total planned trip duration: {totalNights} night{totalNights !== 1 ? "s" : ""}
   170	        </p>
   171	      </div>
   172	    </section>
   173	  );
   174	}===== END: src/components/trip-builder/city-route-planner.tsx =====

    93	function normalizeTransferLabel(value: string) {
    94	  if (value === "Premium Private") return "premium-private";
    95	  if (value === "Private") return "private";
    96	  return "shared";
    97	}
    98	
    99	export function CustomTripFlow(props: Props) {
   100	  const activeStep = useMemo(() => Math.min(Math.max(props.step, 1), 6), [props.step]);
   101	
   102	  const matchingHotels = useMemo(
   103	    () =>
   104	      hotels.filter(
   105	        (hotel) =>
   106	          hotel.destinationId === "dest-bangkok" &&
   107	          hotel.category === props.hotelCategory &&
   108	          hotel.isActive
   109	      ),
   110	    [props.hotelCategory]
   111	  );
   112	
   113	  const matchingTransfers = useMemo(() => {
   114	    const type = normalizeTransferLabel(props.transferType);
   115	
   116	    return transfers.filter(
   117	      (item) =>
   118	        item.destinationIds.includes("dest-bangkok") &&
   119	        item.isActive &&
   120	        item.serviceType === type
   121	    );
   122	  }, [props.transferType]);
   123	
   124	  return (
   125	    <div className="space-y-6">
   126	      <div className="rounded-[28px] border border-slate-200 bg-white p-5 shadow-sm">
   127	        <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-2">
   128	          {steps.map((stepLabel, index) => {
   129	            const number = index + 1;
   130	            const active = number === activeStep;
   131	
   132	            return (
   133	              <button
   134	                key={stepLabel}
   135	                type="button"
   136	                onClick={() => props.onStepChange(number)}
   137	                className={`rounded-full px-4 py-2 text-sm font-medium transition ${
   138	                  active
   139	                    ? "bg-slate-950 text-white"
   140	                    : "bg-slate-100 text-slate-700 hover:bg-slate-200"
   141	                }`}
   142	              >
   143	                {number}. {stepLabel}
   144	              </button>
   145	            );
   146	          })}
   147	        </div>
   148	      </div>
   149	
   150	      {activeStep === 1 ? (
   151	        <div className="space-y-6">
   152	          <DateRangePicker
   153	            checkIn={props.checkIn}
   154	            checkOut={props.checkOut}
   155	            onChange={props.onDatesChange}
   156	          />
   157	          <TravelersSelector
   158	            adults={props.adults}
   159	            children={props.children}
   160	            rooms={props.rooms}
   161	            onChange={props.onTravelersChange}
   162	          />
   163	          <BangkokAreaSelector value={props.area} onChange={props.onAreaChange} />
   164	          <BudgetSelector value={props.budget} onChange={props.onBudgetChange} />
   165	        </div>
   166	      ) : null}
   167	
   168	      {activeStep === 2 ? (
   169	        <div className="rounded-[28px] border border-slate-200 bg-white p-5 shadow-sm">
   170	          <p className="text-lg font-semibold tracking-tight text-slate-950">Choose your stay</p>
   171	          <p className="mt-1 text-sm text-slate-600">
   172	            Pick hotel comfort level first. Matching Bangkok hotels are previewed below.

   178	              return (

   180	                  key={item}
   181	                  type="button"

   183	                  className={`rounded-2xl border p-4 text-left transition ${

   187	                  }`}

   189	                  <p className="text-sm font-semibold text-slate-950">{item}</p>
   190	                </button>
   191	              );
   192	            })}
   193	          </div>
   194	
   195	          <div className="mt-5 grid gap-3 xl:grid-cols-2">
   196	            {matchingHotels.slice(0, 4).map((hotel) => (
   197	              <div
   198	                key={hotel.id}

   200	              >
   201	                <div className="flex items-start justify-between gap-3">

   383	    </div>

===== START: src/components/trip-builder/date-range-picker.tsx =====
     1	"use client";
     2	
     3	import { useMemo } from "react";
     4	import { CalendarDays } from "lucide-react";
     5	
     6	type Props = {
     7	  checkIn: string;
     8	  checkOut: string;
     9	  onChange: (values: { checkIn?: string; checkOut?: string }) => void;
    10	};
    11	
    12	function getNights(checkIn: string, checkOut: string) {
    13	  if (!checkIn || !checkOut) return 0;
    14	
    15	  const start = new Date(checkIn);
    16	  const end = new Date(checkOut);
    17	
    18	  if (Number.isNaN(start.getTime()) || Number.isNaN(end.getTime())) return 0;
    19	
    20	  const diffMs = end.getTime() - start.getTime();
    21	  const diffDays = Math.floor(diffMs / (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24));
    22	
    23	  return diffDays > 0 ? diffDays : 0;
    24	}
    25	
    26	function formatDateLabel(value: string) {
    27	  if (!value) return "";
    28	
    29	  const date = new Date(value);
    30	  if (Number.isNaN(date.getTime())) return value;
    31	
    32	  return date.toLocaleDateString("en-GB", {
    33	    day: "2-digit",
    34	    month: "short",
    35	  });
    36	}
    37	
    38	function getTodayDateString() {
    39	  const today = new Date();
    40	  const year = today.getFullYear();
    41	  const month = `${today.getMonth() + 1}`.padStart(2, "0");
    42	  const day = `${today.getDate()}`.padStart(2, "0");
    43	  return `${year}-${month}-${day}`;
    44	}
    45	
    46	export function DateRangePicker({ checkIn, checkOut, onChange }: Props) {
    47	  const nights = useMemo(() => getNights(checkIn, checkOut), [checkIn, checkOut]);
    48	  const today = useMemo(() => getTodayDateString(), []);
    49	
    50	  const summary = useMemo(() => {
    51	    if (!checkIn || !checkOut || nights <= 0) {
    52	      return "Select check-in and check-out";
    53	    }
    54	
    55	    return `${formatDateLabel(checkIn)} → ${formatDateLabel(checkOut)} · ${nights} Night${
    56	      nights > 1 ? "s" : ""
    57	    }`;
    58	  }, [checkIn, checkOut, nights]);
    59	
    60	  return (
    61	    <div className="rounded-[28px] border border-slate-200 bg-white p-4 shadow-sm">
    62	      <div className="mb-4 flex items-center gap-2">
    63	        <CalendarDays className="h-5 w-5 text-sky-600" />
    64	        <div>
    65	          <p className="text-sm font-semibold text-slate-950">Travel dates</p>
    66	          <p className="text-xs text-slate-500">Trip duration is calculated automatically</p>
    67	        </div>
    68	      </div>
    69	
    70	      <div className="grid gap-4 md:grid-cols-2">
    71	        <label className="block">
    72	          <span className="mb-2 block text-sm font-medium text-slate-700">Check-in</span>
    73	          <input
    74	            type="date"
    75	            min={today}
    76	            value={checkIn}
    77	            onChange={(e) => onChange({ checkIn: e.target.value })}
    78	            className="w-full rounded-2xl border border-slate-200 bg-slate-50 px-4 py-3 text-sm text-slate-950 outline-none transition focus:border-sky-400 focus:bg-white"
    79	          />
    80	        </label>
    81	
    82	        <label className="block">
    83	          <span className="mb-2 block text-sm font-medium text-slate-700">Check-out</span>
    84	          <input
    85	            type="date"
    86	            value={checkOut}
    87	            min={checkIn || today}
    88	            onChange={(e) => onChange({ checkOut: e.target.value })}
    89	            className="w-full rounded-2xl border border-slate-200 bg-slate-50 px-4 py-3 text-sm text-slate-950 outline-none transition focus:border-sky-400 focus:bg-white"
    90	          />
    91	        </label>
    92	      </div>
    93	
    94	      <div className="mt-4 rounded-2xl bg-slate-50 px-4 py-3">
    95	        <p className="text-sm font-medium text-slate-800">{summary}</p>
    96	        <p className="mt-1 text-xs text-slate-500">
    97	          {nights > 0 ? `${nights} Nights · ${nights + 1} Days` : "Trip duration will appear here"}
    98	        </p>
    99	      </div>
   100	    </div>
   101	  );
   102	}===== END: src/components/trip-builder/date-range-picker.tsx =====

===== START: src/components/trip-builder/travelers-selector.tsx =====
     1	"use client";
     2	
     3	type Props = {
     4	  adults: number;
     5	  children: number;
     6	  rooms: number;
     7	  onChange: (values: { adults?: number; children?: number; rooms?: number }) => void;
     8	};
     9	
    10	function Counter({
    11	  label,
    12	  value,
    13	  min = 0,
    14	  onChange,
    15	}: {
    16	  label: string;
    17	  value: number;
    18	  min?: number;
    19	  onChange: (next: number) => void;
    20	}) {
    21	  return (
    22	    <div className="rounded-2xl border border-slate-200 bg-slate-50 p-4">
    23	      <div className="flex items-center justify-between gap-3">
    24	        <span className="text-sm font-medium text-slate-800">{label}</span>
    25	        <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
    26	          <button
    27	            type="button"
    28	            onClick={() => onChange(Math.max(min, value - 1))}
    29	            className="h-9 w-9 rounded-xl border border-slate-200 bg-white text-slate-800"
    30	          >
    31	            -
    32	          </button>
    33	          <span className="w-8 text-center text-sm font-semibold text-slate-950">{value}</span>
    34	          <button
    35	            type="button"
    36	            onClick={() => onChange(value + 1)}
    37	            className="h-9 w-9 rounded-xl border border-slate-200 bg-white text-slate-800"
    38	          >
    39	            +
    40	          </button>
    41	        </div>
    42	      </div>
    43	    </div>
    44	  );
    45	}
    46	
    47	export function TravelersSelector({ adults, children, rooms, onChange }: Props) {
    48	  return (
    49	    <div className="rounded-[28px] border border-slate-200 bg-white p-4 shadow-sm">
    50	      <div className="mb-4">
    51	        <p className="text-sm font-semibold text-slate-950">Who is travelling?</p>
    52	        <p className="text-xs text-slate-500">Set travellers and rooms</p>
    53	      </div>
    54	
    55	      <div className="grid gap-3 md:grid-cols-3">
    56	        <Counter label="Adults" value={adults} min={1} onChange={(next) => onChange({ adults: next })} />
    57	        <Counter label="Children" value={children} min={0} onChange={(next) => onChange({ children: next })} />
    58	        <Counter label="Rooms" value={rooms} min={1} onChange={(next) => onChange({ rooms: next })} />
    59	      </div>
    60	    </div>
    61	  );
    62	}===== END: src/components/trip-builder/travelers-selector.tsx =====
