   441	
   442	function formatINR(value: number) {
   443	  return new Intl.NumberFormat("en-IN", {
   444	    style: "currency",
   445	    currency: "INR",
   446	    maximumFractionDigits: 0,
   447	  }).format(value);
   448	}
   449	
   450	function getTomorrowISODate() {
   451	  const date = new Date();
   452	  date.setDate(date.getDate() + 1);
   453	  return date.toISOString().slice(0, 10);
   454	}
   455	
   456	function formatLongDate(value: string) {
   457	  if (!value) return "Not selected";
   458	  const date = new Date(value);
   459	  if (Number.isNaN(date.getTime())) return value;
   460	
   461	  return new Intl.DateTimeFormat("en-GB", {
   462	    day: "2-digit",
   463	    month: "short",
   464	    year: "numeric",
   465	  }).format(date);
   466	}
   467	
   468	function clampMinimum(value: number, min: number) {
   469	  return Math.max(min, value);
   470	}
   471	
   472	function getTotalTravellers(adults: number, children: number) {
   473	  return adults + children;
   474	}
   475	
   476	function calculatePackagePrice(
   477	  pkg: StandardPackage,
   478	  adults: number,
   479	  children: number,
   480	  rooms: number,
   481	) {
   482	  const adultTotal = pkg.basePricePerPerson * adults;
   483	  const childTotal = Math.round(pkg.basePricePerPerson * 0.72 * children);
   484	  const roomAdjustment = Math.max(0, rooms - 1) * 3500;
   485	  const serviceFee = Math.round((adultTotal + childTotal + roomAdjustment) * 0.05);
   486	
   487	  const total = adultTotal + childTotal + roomAdjustment + serviceFee;
   488	
   489	  return {
   490	    pricePerPerson: pkg.basePricePerPerson,
   491	    totalPrice: Math.round(total),
   492	  };
   493	}
   494	
   495	export function TripBuilderShell() {
   496	  const [mode, setMode] = useState<BuilderMode>("standard");
   497	  const [activeCategory, setActiveCategory] = useState<PackageCategory>("all");
   498	
   499	  const [departureCity, setDepartureCity] = useState("Bangalore");
   500	  const [destinationCity, setDestinationCity] = useState("Bangkok");
   501	  const [departureDate, setDepartureDate] = useState(getTomorrowISODate());
   502	
   503	  const [adults, setAdults] = useState(2);
   504	  const [children, setChildren] = useState(0);
   505	  const [rooms, setRooms] = useState(1);
   506	
   507	  const [selectedPackageId, setSelectedPackageId] = useState<string | null>(null);
   508	  const [detailPackageId, setDetailPackageId] = useState<string | null>(null);
   509	  const [customSeedPackageId, setCustomSeedPackageId] = useState<string | null>(null);
   510	
   511	  const totalTravellers = getTotalTravellers(adults, children);
   512	
   513	  const filteredPackages = useMemo(() => {
   514	    return standardPackages.filter((pkg) =>
   515	      activeCategory === "all" ? true : pkg.category.includes(activeCategory),
   516	    );
   517	  }, [activeCategory]);
   518	
   519	  const packageCards = useMemo(() => {
   520	    return filteredPackages.map((pkg) => ({
   521	      ...pkg,
   522	      pricing: calculatePackagePrice(pkg, adults, children, rooms),
   523	    }));
   524	  }, [filteredPackages, adults, children, rooms]);
   525	
   526	  const selectedPackage =
   527	    packageCards.find((pkg) => pkg.id === selectedPackageId) ?? null;
   528	
   529	  const detailPackage =
   530	    packageCards.find((pkg) => pkg.id === detailPackageId) ?? null;
   531	
   532	  function handleSelectPackage(packageId: string) {
   533	    setSelectedPackageId(packageId);
   534	  }
   535	
   536	  function handleOpenDetail(packageId: string) {
   537	    setDetailPackageId(packageId);
   538	  }
   539	
   540	  function handleCloseDetail() {
   541	    setDetailPackageId(null);
   542	  }
   543	
   544	  function handleCustomizePackage(packageId: string) {
   545	    setSelectedPackageId(packageId);
   546	    setCustomSeedPackageId(packageId);
   547	    setMode("custom");
   548	    setDetailPackageId(null);
   549	  }
   550	
   551	  return (
   552	    <div className="min-h-screen bg-slate-50">
   553	      <header className="sticky top-0 z-40 border-b border-slate-200 bg-white/95 backdrop-blur">
   554	        <div className="mx-auto flex max-w-7xl items-center justify-between px-4 py-4 sm:px-6 lg:px-8">
   555	          <Link href="/" className="flex items-center gap-3">
   556	            <div className="rounded-full bg-sky-100 px-3 py-1 text-[11px] font-semibold uppercase tracking-[0.22em] text-sky-700">
   557	              EasyTrip365
   558	            </div>
   559	            <div className="hidden text-sm font-medium text-slate-600 md:block">
   560	              Thailand Planner
   561	            </div>
   562	          </Link>
   563	
   564	          <nav className="hidden items-center gap-6 md:flex">
   565	            <Link href="/" className="text-sm font-medium text-slate-600 hover:text-slate-950">
   566	              Home
   567	            </Link>
   568	            <Link href="/results" className="text-sm font-medium text-slate-600 hover:text-slate-950">
   569	              Packages
   570	            </Link>
   571	            <Link href="/customize" className="text-sm font-medium text-slate-600 hover:text-slate-950">
   572	              Custom
   573	            </Link>
   574	            <Link href="/review" className="text-sm font-medium text-slate-600 hover:text-slate-950">
   575	              Review
   576	            </Link>
   577	          </nav>
   578	
   579	          <button
   580	            type="button"
   581	            className="inline-flex h-10 w-10 items-center justify-center rounded-full border border-slate-200 bg-white text-slate-700 md:hidden"
   582	            aria-label="Open menu"
   583	          >
   584	            <Menu className="h-5 w-5" />
   585	          </button>
   586	        </div>
   587	      </header>
   588	
   589	      <section className="border-b border-slate-200 bg-[linear-gradient(180deg,#0a2a52_0%,#0d305f_100%)]">
   590	        <div className="mx-auto max-w-7xl px-4 py-5 sm:px-6 lg:px-8">
   591	          <div className="grid gap-3 lg:grid-cols-[1.1fr_1.1fr_1fr_1fr_180px]">
   592	            <SearchField
   593	              label="Starting From"
   594	              value={departureCity}
   595	              onChange={setDepartureCity}
   596	              icon={<MapPin className="h-4 w-4" />}
   597	            />
   598	            <SearchField
   599	              label="Going To"
   600	              value={destinationCity}
   601	              onChange={setDestinationCity}
   602	              icon={<MapPin className="h-4 w-4" />}
   603	            />
   604	            <SearchField
   605	              label="Departure Date"
   606	              value={departureDate}
   607	              onChange={setDepartureDate}
   608	              type="date"
   609	              min={getTomorrowISODate()}
   610	              icon={<CalendarDays className="h-4 w-4" />}
   611	            />
   612	            <GuestsField
   613	              adults={adults}
   614	              children={children}
   615	              rooms={rooms}
   616	              setAdults={setAdults}
   617	              setChildren={setChildren}
   618	              setRooms={setRooms}
   619	            />
   620	            <button
   621	              type="button"
   622	              className="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-2xl bg-sky-500 px-4 py-4 text-sm font-semibold text-white transition hover:bg-sky-600"
   623	            >
   624	              Search
   625	            </button>
   626	          </div>
   627	        </div>
   628	      </section>
   629	
   630	      <main className="mx-auto max-w-7xl px-4 py-6 sm:px-6 lg:px-8">
   631	        <div className="grid gap-4 md:grid-cols-3">
   632	          <ModeCard
   633	            active={mode === "standard"}
   634	            title="Standard Packages"
   635	            description="Curated itineraries with fixed routing and cleaner comparisons."
   636	            onClick={() => setMode("standard")}
   637	            icon={<MapPin className="h-5 w-5" />}
   638	          />
   639	          <ModeCard
   640	            active={mode === "ai"}
   641	            title="AI Guided"
   642	            description="Use AI when the customer wants help choosing a route."
   643	            onClick={() => setMode("ai")}
   644	            icon={<Sparkles className="h-5 w-5" />}
   645	          />
   646	          <ModeCard
   647	            active={mode === "custom"}
   648	            title="Custom Trip"
   649	            description="Build city-night splits like 2N Bangkok · 2N Krabi · 2N Pattaya."
   650	            onClick={() => setMode("custom")}
   651	            icon={<ChevronRight className="h-5 w-5" />}
   652	          />
   653	        </div>
   654	
   655	        {mode === "standard" && (
   656	          <div className="mt-6 space-y-6">
   657	            <section className="overflow-hidden rounded-[30px] border border-slate-200 bg-white shadow-sm">
   658	              <div className="border-b border-slate-200 px-4 py-4 sm:px-6">
   659	                <div className="flex flex-wrap items-center gap-4">
   660	                  {categoryTabs.map((tab) => {
   661	                    const active = activeCategory === tab.value;
   662	
   663	                    return (
   664	                      <button
   665	                        key={tab.value}
   666	                        type="button"
   667	                        onClick={() => setActiveCategory(tab.value)}
   668	                        className={`relative pb-3 text-sm font-semibold transition ${
   669	                          active ? "text-sky-600" : "text-slate-500 hover:text-slate-900"
   670	                        }`}
   671	                      >
   672	                        {tab.label}
   673	                        {active ? (
   674	                          <span className="absolute inset-x-0 bottom-0 h-0.5 rounded-full bg-sky-500" />
   675	                        ) : null}
   676	                      </button>
   677	                    );
   678	                  })}
   679	                </div>
   680	              </div>
   681	
   682	              <div className="grid gap-6 p-4 sm:p-6 xl:grid-cols-[minmax(0,1fr)_340px]">
   683	                <div className="space-y-5">
   684	                  <div className="rounded-3xl border border-slate-200 bg-slate-50 px-4 py-4">
   685	                    <p className="text-sm font-semibold text-slate-900">
   686	                      Recommended Standard Packages
   687	                    </p>
   688	                    <p className="mt-1 text-sm text-slate-500">
   689	                      Showing curated Thailand packages for{" "}
   690	                      <span className="font-semibold text-slate-900">
   691	                        {departureCity}
   692	                      </span>{" "}
   693	                      departing on{" "}
   694	                      <span className="font-semibold text-slate-900">
   695	                        {formatLongDate(departureDate)}
   696	                      </span>
   697	                      .
   698	                    </p>
   699	                  </div>
   700	
   701	                  <div className="grid gap-5 lg:grid-cols-2">
   702	                    {packageCards.map((pkg) => (
   703	                      <article
   704	                        key={pkg.id}
   705	                        className="overflow-hidden rounded-[28px] border border-slate-200 bg-white shadow-sm"
   706	                      >
   707	                        <div
   708	                          className={`h-52 bg-gradient-to-br ${pkg.accentFrom} ${pkg.accentTo} relative`}
   709	                        >
   710	                          <div className="absolute left-4 top-4 rounded-full bg-white/90 px-3 py-1 text-xs font-semibold text-slate-900">
   711	                            {pkg.badge}
   712	                          </div>
   713	                          <div className="absolute bottom-4 left-4 right-4 rounded-2xl bg-white/90 p-3 backdrop-blur">
   714	                            <p className="text-base font-semibold text-slate-950">
   715	                              {pkg.title}
   716	                            </p>
   717	                            <p className="mt-1 text-sm text-slate-600">
   718	                              {pkg.citySplit
   719	                                .map((item) => `${item.nights}N ${item.city}`)
   720	                                .join(" · ")}
   721	                            </p>
   722	                          </div>
   723	                        </div>
   724	
   725	                        <div className="p-5">
   726	                          <p className="text-sm text-slate-600">{pkg.subtitle}</p>
   727	
   728	                          <div className="mt-4 grid grid-cols-2 gap-3 text-sm">
   729	                            <FactPill label={`${pkg.durationNights}N / ${pkg.durationDays}D`} />
   730	                            <FactPill label={pkg.hotelCategory} />
   731	                            <FactPill label={pkg.includedFlights ? "With flights" : "Without flights"} />
   732	                            <FactPill label={`${pkg.activitiesCount} activities`} />
   733	                          </div>
   734	
   735	                          <div className="mt-4 grid gap-2 text-sm text-slate-700 sm:grid-cols-2">
   736	                            <InfoBullet text={pkg.transferType} />
   737	                            <InfoBullet text={pkg.mealsLabel} />
   738	                            {pkg.highlightList.slice(0, 4).map((item) => (
   739	                              <InfoBullet key={item} text={item} />
   740	                            ))}
   741	                          </div>
   742	
   743	                          <div className="mt-4 flex flex-wrap gap-2">
   744	                            {pkg.bestFor.map((item) => (
   745	                              <span
   746	                                key={item}
   747	                                className="rounded-full border border-slate-200 bg-slate-50 px-3 py-1.5 text-xs font-medium text-slate-600"
   748	                              >
   749	                                {item}
   750	                              </span>
   751	                            ))}
   752	                          </div>
   753	
   754	                          <div className="mt-5 rounded-2xl bg-slate-50 p-4">
   755	                            <div className="flex items-end justify-between gap-4">
   756	                              <div>
   757	                                <p className="text-sm text-slate-500">From</p>
   758	                                <p className="text-2xl font-semibold text-slate-950">
   759	                                  {formatINR(pkg.pricing.pricePerPerson)}
   760	                                  <span className="ml-1 text-sm font-medium text-slate-500">
   761	                                    / person
   762	                                  </span>
   763	                                </p>
   764	                              </div>
   765	                              <div className="text-right">
   766	                                <p className="text-sm text-slate-500">Total</p>
   767	                                <p className="text-lg font-semibold text-slate-950">
   768	                                  {formatINR(pkg.pricing.totalPrice)}
   769	                                </p>
   770	                              </div>
   771	                            </div>
   772	                          </div>
   773	
   774	                          <div className="mt-5 grid gap-2 sm:grid-cols-2">
   775	                            <button
   776	                              type="button"
   777	                              onClick={() => handleOpenDetail(pkg.id)}
   778	                              className="rounded-full border border-slate-200 bg-white px-4 py-3 text-sm font-semibold text-slate-700 transition hover:border-slate-300"
   779	                            >
   780	                              View itinerary
   781	                            </button>
   782	                            <button
   783	                              type="button"
   784	                              onClick={() => handleSelectPackage(pkg.id)}
   785	                              className="rounded-full bg-slate-950 px-4 py-3 text-sm font-semibold text-white transition hover:bg-slate-800"
   786	                            >
   787	                              Choose package
   788	                            </button>
   789	                          </div>
   790	
   791	                          <button
   792	                            type="button"
   793	                            onClick={() => handleCustomizePackage(pkg.id)}
   794	                            className="mt-2 w-full rounded-full border border-sky-200 bg-sky-50 px-4 py-3 text-sm font-semibold text-sky-700 transition hover:bg-sky-100"
   795	                          >
   796	                            Customize this package
   797	                          </button>
   798	                        </div>
   799	                      </article>
   800	                    ))}
   801	                  </div>
   802	                </div>
   803	
   804	                <aside className="space-y-4">
   805	                  <div className="rounded-[28px] border border-slate-200 bg-white p-5 shadow-sm">
   806	                    <p className="text-sm font-semibold uppercase tracking-[0.18em] text-sky-600">
   807	                      Trip Summary
   808	                    </p>
   809	                    <div className="mt-4 space-y-3">
   810	                      <SummaryRow label="From" value={departureCity} />
   811	                      <SummaryRow label="Destination" value={destinationCity} />
   812	                      <SummaryRow label="Departure" value={formatLongDate(departureDate)} />
   813	                      <SummaryRow
   814	                        label="Guests"
   815	                        value={`${adults} Adults${children ? `, ${children} Children` : ""}`}
   816	                      />
   817	                      <SummaryRow label="Rooms" value={`${rooms}`} />
   818	                    </div>
   819	
   820	                    {selectedPackage ? (
   821	                      <div className="mt-4 rounded-2xl bg-sky-50 p-4">
   822	                        <p className="text-xs font-semibold uppercase tracking-[0.18em] text-sky-600">
   823	                          Selected package
   824	                        </p>
   825	                        <p className="mt-2 text-lg font-semibold text-slate-950">
   826	                          {selectedPackage.title}
   827	                        </p>
   828	                        <p className="mt-1 text-sm text-slate-600">
   829	                          {selectedPackage.citySplit
   830	                            .map((item) => `${item.nights}N ${item.city}`)
   831	                            .join(" · ")}
   832	                        </p>
   833	                        <p className="mt-3 text-2xl font-semibold text-slate-950">
   834	                          {formatINR(selectedPackage.pricing.totalPrice)}
   835	                        </p>
   836	                      </div>
   837	                    ) : (
   838	                      <div className="mt-4 rounded-2xl border border-dashed border-slate-300 bg-slate-50 p-4 text-sm text-slate-500">
   839	                        No package selected yet.
   840	                      </div>
   841	                    )}
   842	
   843	                    <button
   844	                      type="button"
   845	                      disabled={!selectedPackage}
   846	                      className={`mt-5 w-full rounded-full px-4 py-3 text-sm font-semibold transition ${
   847	                        selectedPackage
   848	                          ? "bg-slate-950 text-white hover:bg-slate-800"
   849	                          : "cursor-not-allowed bg-slate-200 text-slate-500"
   850	                      }`}
   851	                    >
   852	                      Continue booking
   853	                    </button>
   854	                  </div>
   855	
   856	                  <div className="rounded-[28px] border border-sky-200 bg-gradient-to-br from-sky-50 to-cyan-50 p-5">
   857	                    <p className="text-sm font-semibold text-sky-700">
   858	                      Need a different city split?
   859	                    </p>
   860	                    <p className="mt-2 text-sm leading-6 text-slate-600">
   861	                      Standard packages keep the route fixed. The moment a customer
   862	                      wants to change nights, cities, hotels, transfers, or activities,
   863	                      move them into Custom.
   864	                    </p>
   865	                  </div>
   866	                </aside>
   867	              </div>
   868	            </section>
   869	          </div>
   870	        )}
   871	
   872	        {mode === "ai" && (
   873	          <section className="mt-6 rounded-[30px] border border-slate-200 bg-white p-6 shadow-sm">
   874	            <AIGuidedFlow />
   875	          </section>
   876	        )}
   877	
   878	        {mode === "custom" && (
   879	          <section className="mt-6 rounded-[30px] border border-slate-200 bg-white p-6 shadow-sm">
   880	            <div className="mb-4 rounded-3xl border border-sky-200 bg-sky-50 p-4">
   881	              <p className="text-sm font-semibold text-sky-700">Custom mode enabled</p>
   882	              <p className="mt-1 text-sm text-slate-600">
   883	                Build city-night splits like 2N Bangkok · 2N Krabi · 2N Pattaya and
   884	                edit day-level items freely.
   885	              </p>
   886	              {customSeedPackageId ? (
   887	                <p className="mt-2 text-sm text-slate-700">
   888	                  Starting from package:{" "}
   889	                  <span className="font-semibold">
   890	                    {standardPackages.find((pkg) => pkg.id === customSeedPackageId)?.title ??
   891	                      "Selected package"}
   892	                  </span>
   893	                </p>
   894	              ) : null}
   895	            </div>
   896	
   897	            <CustomTripFlow />
   898	          </section>
   899	        )}
   900	      </main>
   901	
   902	      {detailPackage ? (
   903	        <div className="fixed inset-0 z-50 bg-slate-950/50 p-4 backdrop-blur-sm">
   904	          <div className="mx-auto flex h-full max-w-5xl flex-col overflow-hidden rounded-[30px] bg-white shadow-2xl">
   905	            <div className="flex items-start justify-between border-b border-slate-200 px-6 py-5">
   906	              <div>
   907	                <p className="text-sm font-semibold uppercase tracking-[0.18em] text-sky-600">
   908	                  Standard Package Detail
   909	                </p>
   910	                <h2 className="mt-2 text-2xl font-semibold text-slate-950">
   911	                  {detailPackage.title}
   912	                </h2>
   913	                <p className="mt-1 text-sm text-slate-600">
   914	                  {detailPackage.citySplit
   915	                    .map((item) => `${item.nights}N ${item.city}`)
   916	                    .join(" · ")}
   917	                </p>
   918	              </div>
   919	              <button
   920	                type="button"
   921	                onClick={handleCloseDetail}
   922	                className="inline-flex h-10 w-10 items-center justify-center rounded-full border border-slate-200 text-slate-600"
   923	              >
   924	                <X className="h-5 w-5" />
   925	              </button>
   926	            </div>
   927	
   928	            <div className="grid min-h-0 flex-1 gap-0 lg:grid-cols-[minmax(0,1fr)_320px]">
   929	              <div className="overflow-y-auto px-6 py-5">
   930	                <div className={`rounded-[26px] bg-gradient-to-br ${detailPackage.accentFrom} ${detailPackage.accentTo} p-6`}>
   931	                  <p className="text-sm font-semibold text-slate-700">
   932	                    {detailPackage.subtitle}
   933	                  </p>
   934	                  <div className="mt-4 flex flex-wrap gap-2">
   935	                    {detailPackage.citySplit.map((item) => (
   936	                      <span
   937	                        key={`${detailPackage.id}-${item.city}`}
   938	                        className="rounded-full bg-white/85 px-4 py-2 text-sm font-semibold text-slate-900"
   939	                      >
   940	                        {item.nights}N {item.city}
   941	                      </span>
   942	                    ))}
   943	                  </div>
   944	                </div>
   945	
   946	                <div className="mt-6 grid gap-4 sm:grid-cols-3">
   947	                  <DetailInfoCard label="Hotel" value={detailPackage.hotelCategory} />
   948	                  <DetailInfoCard label="Transfers" value={detailPackage.transferType} />
   949	                  <DetailInfoCard
   950	                    label="Meals"
   951	                    value={detailPackage.mealsLabel}
   952	                  />
   953	                </div>
   954	
   955	                <div className="mt-6">
   956	                  <p className="text-lg font-semibold text-slate-950">Day-wise itinerary</p>
   957	                  <p className="mt-1 text-sm text-slate-500">
   958	                    This is the standard plan. Editing any day should move the trip into Custom.
   959	                  </p>
   960	
   961	                  <div className="mt-5 space-y-4">
   962	                    {detailPackage.dayPlan.map((item) => (
   963	                      <div
   964	                        key={`${detailPackage.id}-day-${item.day}`}
   965	                        className="rounded-[24px] border border-slate-200 bg-white p-5"
   966	                      >
   967	                        <div className="flex flex-col gap-4 sm:flex-row sm:items-start sm:justify-between">
   968	                          <div>
   969	                            <div className="inline-flex rounded-full bg-orange-50 px-3 py-1 text-xs font-semibold text-orange-700">
   970	                              Day {item.day}
   971	                            </div>
   972	                            <h3 className="mt-3 text-lg font-semibold text-slate-950">
   973	                              {item.title}
   974	                            </h3>
   975	                            <p className="mt-1 text-sm font-medium text-sky-700">
   976	                              {item.city}
   977	                            </p>
   978	                            <p className="mt-3 text-sm leading-6 text-slate-600">
   979	                              {item.description}
   980	                            </p>
   981	                          </div>
   982	
   983	                          <div className="flex gap-2">
   984	                            <button
   985	                              type="button"
   986	                              onClick={() => handleCustomizePackage(detailPackage.id)}
   987	                              className="rounded-full border border-slate-200 bg-white px-4 py-2 text-xs font-semibold text-slate-700"
   988	                            >
   989	                              Modify day
   990	                            </button>
   991	                          </div>
   992	                        </div>
   993	
   994	                        <div className="mt-4 grid gap-2 text-sm text-slate-700 sm:grid-cols-2">
   995	                          {item.transfer ? <InfoBullet text={item.transfer} /> : null}
   996	                          {item.hotel ? <InfoBullet text={item.hotel} /> : null}
   997	                          {item.activities?.map((activity) => (
   998	                            <InfoBullet key={activity} text={activity} />
   999	                          ))}
  1000	                          {item.meals?.map((meal) => (
  1001	                            <InfoBullet key={meal} text={meal} />
  1002	                          ))}
  1003	                        </div>
  1004	                      </div>
  1005	                    ))}
  1006	                  </div>
  1007	                </div>
  1008	              </div>
  1009	
  1010	              <aside className="border-l border-slate-200 bg-slate-50 px-5 py-5">
  1011	                <div className="rounded-[24px] border border-slate-200 bg-white p-5">
  1012	                  <p className="text-xs font-semibold uppercase tracking-[0.18em] text-sky-600">
  1013	                    Current estimate
  1014	                  </p>
  1015	                  <p className="mt-3 text-3xl font-semibold text-slate-950">
  1016	                    {formatINR(detailPackage.pricing.totalPrice)}
  1017	                  </p>
  1018	                  <p className="mt-1 text-sm text-slate-500">
  1019	                    {formatINR(detailPackage.pricing.pricePerPerson)} / person
  1020	                  </p>
  1021	
  1022	                  <div className="mt-4 space-y-3">
  1023	                    <SummaryRow label="Departure" value={formatLongDate(departureDate)} />
  1024	                    <SummaryRow label="Guests" value={`${totalTravellers}`} />
  1025	                    <SummaryRow label="Rooms" value={`${rooms}`} />
  1026	                  </div>
  1027	
  1028	                  <div className="mt-5 grid gap-2">
  1029	                    <button
  1030	                      type="button"
  1031	                      onClick={() => {
  1032	                        handleSelectPackage(detailPackage.id);
  1033	                        handleCloseDetail();
  1034	                      }}
  1035	                      className="rounded-full bg-slate-950 px-4 py-3 text-sm font-semibold text-white transition hover:bg-slate-800"
  1036	                    >
  1037	                      Choose this package
  1038	                    </button>
  1039	                    <button
  1040	                      type="button"
  1041	                      onClick={() => handleCustomizePackage(detailPackage.id)}
  1042	                      className="rounded-full border border-sky-200 bg-sky-50 px-4 py-3 text-sm font-semibold text-sky-700 transition hover:bg-sky-100"
  1043	                    >
  1044	                      Customize this package
  1045	                    </button>
  1046	                  </div>
  1047	                </div>
  1048	              </aside>
  1049	            </div>
  1050	          </div>
  1051	        </div>
  1052	      ) : null}
  1053	    </div>
  1054	  );
  1055	}
  1056	
  1057	function SearchField({
  1058	  label,
  1059	  value,
  1060	  onChange,
  1061	  type = "text",
  1062	  min,
  1063	  icon,
  1064	}: {
  1065	  label: string;
  1066	  value: string;
  1067	  onChange: (value: string) => void;
  1068	  type?: "text" | "date";
  1069	  min?: string;
  1070	  icon: React.ReactNode;
  1071	}) {
  1072	  return (
  1073	    <label className="rounded-2xl bg-white/10 px-4 py-3 text-white">
  1074	      <span className="mb-1 flex items-center gap-2 text-[11px] font-semibold uppercase tracking-[0.18em] text-sky-100">
  1075	        {icon}
  1076	        {label}
  1077	      </span>
  1078	      <input
  1079	        type={type}
  1080	        value={value}
  1081	        min={min}
  1082	        onChange={(e) => onChange(e.target.value)}
  1083	        className="w-full bg-transparent text-base font-medium text-white outline-none [color-scheme:dark]"
  1084	      />
  1085	    </label>
  1086	  );
  1087	}
  1088	
  1089	function GuestsField({
  1090	  adults,
  1091	  children,
  1092	  rooms,
  1093	  setAdults,
  1094	  setChildren,
  1095	  setRooms,
  1096	}: {
  1097	  adults: number;
  1098	  children: number;
  1099	  rooms: number;
  1100	  setAdults: (value: number) => void;
  1101	  setChildren: (value: number) => void;
  1102	  setRooms: (value: number) => void;
  1103	}) {
  1104	  return (
  1105	    <div className="rounded-2xl bg-white/10 px-4 py-3 text-white">
  1106	      <div className="mb-1 flex items-center gap-2 text-[11px] font-semibold uppercase tracking-[0.18em] text-sky-100">
  1107	        <Users className="h-4 w-4" />
  1108	        Rooms & Guests
  1109	      </div>
  1110	      <div className="grid grid-cols-3 gap-2">
  1111	        <CounterMini
  1112	          label="A"
  1113	          value={adults}
  1114	          onMinus={() => setAdults(clampMinimum(adults - 1, 1))}
  1115	          onPlus={() => setAdults(adults + 1)}
  1116	        />
  1117	        <CounterMini
  1118	          label="C"
  1119	          value={children}
  1120	          onMinus={() => setChildren(clampMinimum(children - 1, 0))}
  1121	          onPlus={() => setChildren(children + 1)}
  1122	        />
  1123	        <CounterMini
  1124	          label="R"
  1125	          value={rooms}
  1126	          onMinus={() => setRooms(clampMinimum(rooms - 1, 1))}
  1127	          onPlus={() => setRooms(rooms + 1)}
  1128	        />
  1129	      </div>
  1130	    </div>
  1131	  );
  1132	}
  1133	
  1134	function CounterMini({
  1135	  label,
  1136	  value,
  1137	  onMinus,
  1138	  onPlus,
  1139	}: {
  1140	  label: string;
  1141	  value: number;
  1142	  onMinus: () => void;
  1143	  onPlus: () => void;
  1144	}) {
  1145	  return (
  1146	    <div className="rounded-xl bg-white/10 px-2 py-2">
  1147	      <div className="mb-1 text-center text-[10px] font-semibold uppercase tracking-[0.18em] text-sky-100">
  1148	        {label}
  1149	      </div>
  1150	      <div className="flex items-center justify-between gap-1">
  1151	        <button
  1152	          type="button"
  1153	          onClick={onMinus}
  1154	          className="inline-flex h-6 w-6 items-center justify-center rounded-full bg-white/10"
  1155	        >
  1156	          <Minus className="h-3 w-3" />
  1157	        </button>
  1158	        <span className="text-sm font-semibold">{value}</span>
  1159	        <button
  1160	          type="button"
  1161	          onClick={onPlus}
  1162	          className="inline-flex h-6 w-6 items-center justify-center rounded-full bg-white/10"
  1163	        >
  1164	          <Plus className="h-3 w-3" />
  1165	        </button>
  1166	      </div>
  1167	    </div>
  1168	  );
  1169	}
  1170

===== START: src/components/public/ai-helper-widget.tsx =====
     1	"use client";
     2	
     3	import { useEffect, useMemo, useState } from "react";
     4	import { Search, Sparkles, Wand2 } from "lucide-react";
     5	
     6	const prompts = [
     7	  "Plan your next dream vacation...",
     8	  "Where do you want to go?",
     9	  "Type your destination...",
    10	  "Find your perfect getaway...",
    11	  "Let AI help you plan faster...",
    12	];
    13	
    14	type AiHelperWidgetProps = {
    15	  className?: string;
    16	  compact?: boolean;
    17	};
    18	
    19	export function AiHelperWidget({
    20	  className = "",
    21	  compact = false,
    22	}: AiHelperWidgetProps) {
    23	  const [activeIndex, setActiveIndex] = useState(0);
    24	  const [displayedText, setDisplayedText] = useState("");
    25	  const activePrompt = useMemo(() => prompts[activeIndex], [activeIndex]);
    26	
    27	  useEffect(() => {
    28	    let current = 0;
    29	    setDisplayedText("");
    30	
    31	    const typingInterval = setInterval(() => {
    32	      current += 1;
    33	      setDisplayedText(activePrompt.slice(0, current));
    34	
    35	      if (current >= activePrompt.length) {
    36	        clearInterval(typingInterval);
    37	      }
    38	    }, 30);
    39	
    40	    return () => clearInterval(typingInterval);
    41	  }, [activePrompt]);
    42	
    43	  useEffect(() => {
    44	    const interval = setInterval(() => {
    45	      setActiveIndex((prev) => (prev + 1) % prompts.length);
    46	    }, 2600);
    47	
    48	    return () => clearInterval(interval);
    49	  }, []);
    50	
    51	  return (
    52	    <div
    53	      className={`ai-widget-shell group relative overflow-hidden rounded-[18px] p-[1.5px] ${
    54	        compact ? "min-h-[54px]" : "min-h-[72px]"
    55	      } ${className}`}
    56	    >
    57	      <div className="ai-widget-inner relative h-full rounded-[16px] bg-[linear-gradient(135deg,rgba(255,255,255,0.97),rgba(248,250,252,0.94))] px-3 py-2 backdrop-blur-xl sm:px-4">
    58	        <div className="pointer-events-none absolute inset-0 rounded-[16px] bg-[radial-gradient(circle_at_top_left,rgba(255,255,255,0.95),transparent_34%),radial-gradient(circle_at_bottom_right,rgba(59,130,246,0.10),transparent_36%)]" />
    59	        <div className="ai-widget-shine pointer-events-none absolute -left-20 top-0 h-full w-16 rotate-12 bg-white/50 blur-xl" />
    60	
    61	        <div className="relative z-10 flex items-center gap-2">
    62	          <div className="relative flex h-7 w-7 shrink-0 items-center justify-center rounded-xl bg-slate-950 text-white shadow-[0_8px_18px_rgba(15,23,42,0.18)] sm:h-8 sm:w-8">
    63	            <div className="absolute inset-0 rounded-xl bg-sky-400/25 blur-md animate-pulse" />
    64	            <Sparkles className="relative h-3.5 w-3.5 animate-pulse" />
    65	          </div>
    66	
    67	          <div className="min-w-0 flex-1">
    68	            <div className="mb-0.5 flex items-center gap-2">
    69	              <span className="inline-flex items-center gap-1 rounded-full bg-sky-50 px-2 py-0.5 text-[8px] font-semibold uppercase tracking-[0.2em] text-sky-700">
    70	                <Wand2 className="h-2.5 w-2.5" />
    71	                AI Trip Assist
    72	              </span>
    73	            </div>
    74	
    75	            <div className="truncate text-[11px] font-semibold leading-4 text-slate-900 sm:text-[12px]">
    76	              {displayedText}
    77	              <span className="ml-0.5 inline-block h-3 w-[1.5px] translate-y-[2px] bg-slate-900 animate-pulse" />
    78	            </div>
    79	
    80	            {!compact ? (
    81	              <p className="mt-0.5 line-clamp-1 text-[10px] leading-4 text-slate-500">
    82	                Smart suggestions, destinations, and quick itinerary ideas.
    83	              </p>
    84	            ) : null}
    85	          </div>
    86	
    87	          <div className="relative flex h-7 w-7 shrink-0 items-center justify-center rounded-xl bg-gradient-to-br from-amber-400 via-yellow-300 to-orange-400 text-slate-950 shadow-[0_10px_18px_rgba(251,191,36,0.28)] sm:h-8 sm:w-8">
    88	            <div className="absolute inset-0 rounded-xl bg-yellow-300/40 blur-md animate-pulse" />
    89	            <Search className="ai-search-icon relative h-3.5 w-3.5" />
    90	          </div>
    91	        </div>
    92	      </div>
    93	    </div>
    94	  );
    95	}===== END: src/components/public/ai-helper-widget.tsx =====

   114	export function FaqSection() {
   115	  const [activeGroup, setActiveGroup] = useState(faqGroups[0].key);
   116	  const currentGroup =
   117	    faqGroups.find((group) => group.key === activeGroup) ?? faqGroups[0];
   118	
   119	  const initialOpen = useMemo(() => currentGroup.faqs[0]?.question ?? "", [currentGroup]);
   120	  const [openQuestion, setOpenQuestion] = useState(initialOpen);
   121	
   122	  if (openQuestion !== initialOpen && !currentGroup.faqs.some((faq) => faq.question === openQuestion)) {
   123	    setOpenQuestion(initialOpen);
   124	  }
   125	
   126	  return (
   127	    <section className="py-16 sm:py-20 lg:py-24">
   128	      <div className="mx-auto max-w-7xl px-4 sm:px-6 lg:px-8">
   129	        <div className="relative overflow-hidden rounded-[36px] border border-slate-200 bg-[linear-gradient(135deg,rgba(255,247,247,0.95)_0%,rgba(243,247,255,0.94)_45%,rgba(232,250,255,0.96)_100%)] p-6 shadow-[0_24px_80px_rgba(15,23,42,0.06)] sm:p-8 lg:p-12">
   130	          <div className="pointer-events-none absolute inset-0 bg-[radial-gradient(circle_at_18%_72%,rgba(251,146,60,0.10),transparent_22%),radial-gradient(circle_at_78%_26%,rgba(56,189,248,0.12),transparent_24%),radial-gradient(circle_at_50%_88%,rgba(167,139,250,0.10),transparent_18%)]" />
   131	          <div className="pointer-events-none absolute left-[18%] top-[18%] h-4 w-4 rounded-full bg-sky-300/80" />
   132	          <div className="pointer-events-none absolute left-[52%] top-[8%] h-5 w-5 rounded-full bg-indigo-300/80" />
   133	          <div className="pointer-events-none absolute right-[14%] top-[24%] h-7 w-7 rounded-full bg-cyan-200/90" />
   134	          <div className="pointer-events-none absolute right-[4%] top-[22%] h-2 w-2 rounded-full bg-sky-300/80" />
   135	          <div className="pointer-events-none absolute left-[24%] bottom-[8%] h-3 w-3 rounded-full bg-indigo-300/70" />
   136	
   137	          <div className="relative">
   138	            <div className="mx-auto max-w-3xl text-center">
   139	              <span className="inline-flex rounded-full border border-slate-200 bg-white/70 px-3 py-1 text-[10px] font-semibold uppercase tracking-[0.22em] text-slate-600">
   140	                FAQ
   141	              </span>
   142	
   143	              <h2 className="mt-4 text-3xl font-semibold tracking-tight text-slate-950 sm:text-4xl lg:text-5xl">
   144	                Frequently Asked Questions
   145	              </h2>
   146	
   147	              <p className="mx-auto mt-4 max-w-2xl text-sm leading-7 text-slate-600 sm:text-base">
   148	                Common questions about planning, comparing packages, customization,
   149	                and how the booking flow is designed to stay clean and easy to use.
   150	              </p>
   151	            </div>
   152	
   153	            <div className="mt-10 grid gap-6 lg:grid-cols-[0.9fr_1.25fr]">
   154	              <div className="space-y-4">
   155	                {faqGroups.map((group) => {
   156	                  const active = group.key === activeGroup;
   157	
   158	                  return (
   159	                    <button
   160	                      key={group.key}
   161	                      type="button"
   162	                      onClick={() => {
   163	                        setActiveGroup(group.key);
   164	                        setOpenQuestion(group.faqs[0]?.question ?? "");
   165	                      }}
   166	                      className={`flex w-full items-center justify-between rounded-[18px] border px-5 py-5 text-left transition ${
   167	                        active
   168	                          ? "border-slate-200 bg-white text-slate-950 shadow-[0_14px_32px_rgba(15,23,42,0.06)]"
   169	                          : "border-slate-200/80 bg-white/55 text-slate-500 hover:bg-white/80"
   170	                      }`}
   171	                    >
   172	                      <span className="text-base font-medium">{group.label}</span>
   173	                      <ChevronRight
   174	                        className={`h-5 w-5 transition ${
   175	                          active ? "text-slate-900" : "text-slate-400"
   176	                        }`}
   177	                      />
   178	                    </button>
   179	                  );
   180	                })}
   181	              </div>
   182	
   183	              <div className="space-y-4">
   184	                {currentGroup.faqs.map((faq, index) => {
   185	                  const open = faq.question === openQuestion;
   186	
   187	                  return (
   188	                    <div
   189	                      key={faq.question}
   190	                      className={`overflow-hidden rounded-[18px] border transition ${
   191	                        open
   192	                          ? "border-slate-200 bg-white shadow-[0_14px_32px_rgba(15,23,42,0.06)]"
   193	                          : "border-slate-200/90 bg-white/50"
   194	                      }`}
   195	                    >
   196	                      <button
   197	                        type="button"
   198	                        onClick={() =>
   199	                          setOpenQuestion(open ? "" : faq.question)
   200	                        }
   201	                        className="flex w-full items-start justify-between gap-4 px-5 py-5 text-left"
   202	                      >
   203	                        <span className="pr-2 text-base font-medium leading-7 text-slate-900">
   204	                          {faq.question}
   205	                        </span>
   206	
   207	                        <span className="mt-0.5 shrink-0 text-slate-900">
   208	                          {open ? <X className="h-6 w-6" /> : <Plus className="h-6 w-6" />}
   209	                        </span>
   210	                      </button>
   211	
   212	                      <div
   213	                        className={`grid transition-all duration-300 ease-out ${
   214	                          open ? "grid-rows-[1fr]" : "grid-rows-[0fr]"
   215	                        }`}
   216	                      >
   217	                        <div className="overflow-hidden">
   218	                          <div className="px-5 pb-5 text-sm leading-7 text-slate-600 sm:text-base">
   219	                            {faq.answer}
   220	                          </div>
   221	                        </div>
   222	                      </div>
   223	
   224	                      {!open && index !== currentGroup.faqs.length - 1 ? null : null}
   225	                    </div>
   226	                  );
   227	                })}
   228	              </div>
   229	            </div>
   230	          </div>
   231	        </div>
   232	      </div>
   233	    </section>
   234	  );
   235	}===== END: src/components/public/faq-section.tsx =====

===== START: src/components/public/live-price-sidebar.tsx =====
     1	import { Wallet, ArrowUpRight, BadgeIndianRupee } from "lucide-react";
     2	import { formatCurrency } from "@/lib/helpers/format";
     3	
     4	type LivePriceSidebarProps = {
     5	  selectedPackagePrice: number;
     6	  serviceFee: number;
     7	  travelStyle: string;
     8	};
     9	
    10	function getPlanningMultiplier(travelStyle: string) {
    11	  const value = travelStyle.toLowerCase();
    12	
    13	  if (value.includes("luxury")) return 1.28;
    14	  if (value.includes("honeymoon")) return 1.18;
    15	  if (value.includes("family")) return 1.12;
    16	  if (value.includes("adventure")) return 1.1;
    17	  if (value.includes("budget")) return 0.92;
    18	
    19	  return 1;
    20	}
    21	
    22	export function LivePriceSidebar({
    23	  selectedPackagePrice,
    24	  serviceFee,
    25	  travelStyle,
    26	}: LivePriceSidebarProps) {
    27	  const styleMultiplier = getPlanningMultiplier(travelStyle);
    28	  const planningEstimate = Math.round(selectedPackagePrice * styleMultiplier);
    29	  const estimatedTotal = planningEstimate + serviceFee;
    30	
    31	  return (
    32	    <div className="overflow-hidden rounded-[30px] border border-slate-200 bg-white shadow-[0_20px_50px_rgba(15,23,42,0.06)]">
    33	      <div className="bg-[linear-gradient(135deg,#0f172a_0%,#1d4ed8_100%)] p-5 text-white sm:p-6">
    34	        <div className="flex items-start justify-between gap-3">
    35	          <div>
    36	            <p className="text-[11px] font-semibold uppercase tracking-[0.22em] text-white/70">
    37	              Planning Estimate
    38	            </p>
    39	            <h3 className="mt-2 text-2xl font-semibold tracking-tight">
    40	              {formatCurrency(estimatedTotal)}
    41	            </h3>
    42	            <p className="mt-2 text-sm leading-6 text-white/80">
    43	              Early estimate based on your current trip style and saved base package.
    44	            </p>
    45	          </div>
    46	
    47	          <span className="inline-flex h-11 w-11 items-center justify-center rounded-2xl bg-white/10">
    48	            <Wallet className="h-5 w-5" />
    49	          </span>
    50	        </div>
    51	      </div>
    52	
    53	      <div className="space-y-4 p-5 sm:p-6">
    54	        <div className="flex items-center justify-between text-sm">
    55	          <span className="text-slate-500">Saved base package</span>
    56	          <span className="font-semibold text-slate-900">
    57	            {formatCurrency(selectedPackagePrice)}
    58	          </span>
    59	        </div>
    60	
    61	        <div className="flex items-center justify-between text-sm">
    62	          <span className="text-slate-500">Style-led planning impact</span>
    63	          <span className="font-semibold text-slate-900">
    64	            {formatCurrency(planningEstimate - selectedPackagePrice)}
    65	          </span>
    66	        </div>
    67	
    68	        <div className="flex items-center justify-between text-sm">
    69	          <span className="text-slate-500">Service fee</span>
    70	          <span className="font-semibold text-slate-900">
    71	            {formatCurrency(serviceFee)}
    72	          </span>
    73	        </div>
    74	
    75	        <div className="rounded-[22px] bg-slate-50 p-4">
    76	          <div className="flex items-start gap-3">
    77	            <span className="inline-flex h-10 w-10 items-center justify-center rounded-2xl bg-white text-slate-700 shadow-sm">
    78	              <BadgeIndianRupee className="h-4 w-4" />
    79	            </span>
    80	            <div>
    81	              <p className="text-sm font-semibold text-slate-900">
    82	                Better-fit options will show next
    83	              </p>
    84	              <p className="mt-1 text-sm leading-6 text-slate-600">
    85	                In Results, we’ll prioritize stronger-fit packages, best-value picks,
    86	                and worthwhile upgrades instead of dumping random options.
    87	              </p>
    88	            </div>
    89	          </div>
    90	        </div>
    91	
    92	        <div className="inline-flex items-center gap-2 rounded-full border border-slate-200 bg-white px-3 py-2 text-xs font-semibold uppercase tracking-[0.18em] text-slate-600">
    93	          <ArrowUpRight className="h-3.5 w-3.5" />
    94	          {travelStyle || "Balanced"} planning mode
    95	        </div>
    96	      </div>
    97	    </div>
    98	  );

===== START: src/components/public/public-header.tsx =====
     1	"use client";
     2	
     3	import Link from "next/link";
     4	import { useEffect, useRef, useState } from "react";
     5	
     6	const navItems = [
     7	  { label: "Destinations", href: "/results" },
     8	  { label: "Packages", href: "/results" },
     9	  { label: "Plan Your Trip", href: "/trip-builder" },
    10	  { label: "Contact", href: "/" },
    11	];
    12	
    13	export function PublicHeader() {
    14	  const [visible, setVisible] = useState(true);
    15	  const lastY = useRef(0);
    16	
    17	  useEffect(() => {
    18	    const onScroll = () => {
    19	      const currentY = window.scrollY;
    20	
    21	      if (currentY < 20) {
    22	        setVisible(true);
    23	        lastY.current = currentY;
    24	        return;
    25	      }
    26	
    27	      if (currentY > lastY.current && currentY > 80) {
    28	        setVisible(false);
    29	      } else {
    30	        setVisible(true);
    31	      }
    32	
    33	      lastY.current = currentY;
    34	    };
    35	
    36	    window.addEventListener("scroll", onScroll, { passive: true });
    37	    return () => window.removeEventListener("scroll", onScroll);
    38	  }, []);
    39	
    40	  return (
    41	    <header
    42	      className={`fixed inset-x-0 top-3 z-[70] px-3 transition-all duration-300 sm:top-5 sm:px-5 ${
    43	        visible
    44	          ? "translate-y-0 opacity-100"
    45	          : "-translate-y-5 pointer-events-none opacity-0"
    46	      }`}
    47	    >
    48	      <div className="mx-auto max-w-7xl">
    49	        <div className="flex items-center justify-between rounded-[30px] bg-[#f6f1e8]/72 px-4 py-3 backdrop-blur-xl sm:px-6">
    50	          <Link href="/" className="flex items-center gap-3">
    51	            <div className="flex h-10 w-10 items-center justify-center rounded-2xl bg-[linear-gradient(135deg,#0f172a_0%,#f97316_100%)] text-xs font-bold text-white shadow-[0_10px_24px_rgba(15,23,42,0.18)]">
    52	              ET
    53	            </div>
    54	            <div>
    55	              <p className="text-[11px] font-semibold tracking-[0.18em] text-slate-900 sm:text-xs">
    56	                EASYTRIP365
    57	              </p>
    58	              <p className="text-[10px] text-slate-500 sm:text-xs">
    59	                Curated holiday journeys
    60	              </p>
    61	            </div>
    62	          </Link>
    63	
    64	          <nav className="hidden items-center gap-3 lg:flex">
    65	            {navItems.map((item) => (
    66	              <Link
    67	                key={item.label}
    68	                href={item.href}
    69	                className="rounded-full border border-black/70 bg-transparent px-5 py-2.5 text-sm font-medium text-slate-800 transition hover:border-black hover:text-slate-950"
    70	              >
    71	                {item.label}
    72	              </Link>
    73	            ))}
    74	          </nav>
    75	
    76	          <Link
    77	            href="/trip-builder"
    78	            className="inline-flex rounded-full bg-orange-500 px-5 py-2.5 text-sm font-semibold text-white shadow-[0_14px_30px_rgba(249,115,22,0.28)] transition hover:bg-orange-600"
    79	          >
    80	            Start Planning
    81	          </Link>
    82	        </div>
    83	      </div>
    84	    </header>
    85	  );
    86	}

     1	const travelStyleOptions = [
     2	  "Leisure",
     3	  "Premium Leisure",
     4	  "Luxury Escape",
     5	  "Fast-Paced Explorer",
     6	];
     7	
     8	type TravelStyleSelectorProps = {
     9	  value: string;
    10	  onChange?: (value: string) => void;
    11	};
    12	
    13	export function TravelStyleSelector({
    14	  value,
    15	  onChange,
    16	}: TravelStyleSelectorProps) {
    17	  return (
    18	    <div className="grid gap-3 md:grid-cols-2">
    19	      {travelStyleOptions.map((option) => {
    20	        const active = value === option;
    21	
    22	        return (
    23	          <button
    24	            key={option}
    25	            type="button"
    26	            onClick={() => onChange?.(option)}
    27	            className={`rounded-3xl border p-4 text-left transition ${
    28	              active
    29	                ? "border-black bg-black text-white"
    30	                : "border-neutral-200 bg-white text-neutral-900 hover:border-neutral-400"
    31	            }`}
    32	          >
    33	            <p className="text-sm font-bold">{option}</p>
    34	          </button>
    35	        );
    36	      })}
    37	    </div>
    38	  );

===== START: src/components/public/trip-builder-stepper.tsx =====
     1	type TripBuilderStepperProps = {
     2	  currentStep: number;
     3	};
     4	
     5	const steps = [
     6	  { number: "01", label: "Choose" },
     7	  { number: "02", label: "Results" },
     8	  { number: "03", label: "Customize" },
     9	  { number: "04", label: "Review" },
    10	  { number: "05", label: "Confirm" },
    11	];
    12	
    13	export function TripBuilderStepper({
    14	  currentStep,
    15	}: TripBuilderStepperProps) {
    16	  return (
    17	    <div className="rounded-[28px] border border-white/70 bg-white/75 p-3 shadow-[0_18px_50px_rgba(15,23,42,0.06)] backdrop-blur">
    18	      <div className="grid gap-2 md:grid-cols-5">
    19	        {steps.map((step, index) => {
    20	          const stepNumber = index + 1;
    21	          const isActive = stepNumber === currentStep;
    22	          const isComplete = stepNumber < currentStep;
    23	
    24	          return (
    25	            <div
    26	              key={step.label}
    27	              className={`rounded-[22px] border px-4 py-3 transition ${
    28	                isActive
    29	                  ? "border-slate-950 bg-slate-950 text-white shadow-[0_16px_34px_rgba(15,23,42,0.20)]"
    30	                  : isComplete
    31	                  ? "border-emerald-200 bg-emerald-50 text-emerald-800"
    32	                  : "border-slate-200 bg-white text-slate-500"
    33	              }`}
    34	            >
    35	              <p
    36	                className={`text-[11px] font-semibold uppercase tracking-[0.22em] ${
    37	                  isActive ? "text-white/70" : isComplete ? "text-emerald-600" : "text-slate-400"
    38	                }`}
    39	              >
    40	                {step.number}
    41	              </p>
    42	              <p className="mt-1 text-sm font-semibold">{step.label}</p>
    43	            </div>
    44	          );
    45	        })}
    46	      </div>
    47	    </div>
    48	  );
    49	}===== END: src/components/public/trip-builder-stepper.tsx =====

    27	        {points.map((point) => (

    31	          >
    32	            <span className="mt-0.5 inline-flex h-8 w-8 items-center justify-center rounded-xl bg-orange-50 text-orange-600">
    33	              <BadgeCheck className="h-4 w-4" />
    34	            </span>
    35	            <p className="text-sm leading-6 text-slate-700">{point}</p>
    36	          </div>
    37	        ))}
    38	      </div>
    39	
    40	      <div className="mt-5 rounded-[22px] bg-slate-950 p-4 text-white">
    41	        <div className="flex items-start gap-3">
    42	          <span className="inline-flex h-10 w-10 items-center justify-center rounded-2xl bg-white/10">
    43	            <Sparkles className="h-4 w-4" />
    44	          </span>
    45	          <div>
    46	            <p className="text-sm font-semibold">Commercially smart, customer-safe</p>
    47	            <p className="mt-1 text-sm leading-6 text-white/75">
    48	              EasyTrip should surface stronger options, but always with fit-first guidance.
    49	            </p>
    50	          </div>
    51	        </div>
    52	      </div>
    53	    </div>
    54	  );

    53	  return (
    54	    <span className="inline-flex w-fit rounded-full border border-slate-300/80 bg-white/90 px-3 py-1.5 text-[10px] font-semibold text-slate-700 shadow-[0_10px_24px_rgba(15,23,42,0.08)] backdrop-blur md:text-[11px]">

    60	function MetaPill({
    61	  value,
    62	  label,
    63	}: {
    64	  value: string;
    65	  label: string;
    66	}) {

    68	    <div className="rounded-[14px] border border-white/12 bg-white/10 px-3 py-2.5 backdrop-blur-xl">
    69	      <p className="text-sm font-semibold text-white">{value}</p>

    71	        {label}
    72	      </p>
    73	    </div>
    74	  );
    75	}

    77	export function WhyChooseUsGrid() {
    78	  const sectionRef = useRef<HTMLElement | null>(null);
    79	  const [isOpen, setIsOpen] = useState(false);
    80	
    81	  useEffect(() => {
    82	    const node = sectionRef.current;
    83	    if (!node) return;
    84	
    85	    const observer = new IntersectionObserver(
    86	      ([entry]) => {
    87	        setIsOpen(entry.isIntersecting && entry.intersectionRatio > 0.42);
    88	      },
    89	      {
    90	        threshold: [0.2, 0.42, 0.6],
    91	      }
    92	    );
    93	
    94	    observer.observe(node);
    95	    return () => observer.disconnect();
    96	  }, []);
    97	
    98	  return (
    99	    <section
   100	      ref={sectionRef}
   101	      className="overflow-hidden rounded-[34px] border border-slate-200 bg-[linear-gradient(180deg,#f7fbfb_0%,#eff5f4_55%,#f7f7f4_100%)] px-4 py-8 shadow-[0_20px_60px_rgba(15,23,42,0.06)] sm:px-6 sm:py-10 lg:px-8 lg:py-12"
   102	    >
   103	      <div className="mx-auto max-w-6xl">
   104	        <div className="text-center">
   105	          <span className="inline-flex rounded-full border border-slate-200 bg-white/80 px-3 py-1 text-[10px] font-semibold uppercase tracking-[0.22em] text-slate-600">
   106	            How EasyTrip365 works
   107	          </span>
   108	
   109	          <h3 className="mt-4 text-3xl font-semibold tracking-tight text-slate-950 sm:text-4xl">
   110	            Three ways. One smarter booking flow.
   111	          </h3>
   112	
   113	          <p className="mx-auto mt-3 max-w-2xl text-sm leading-6 text-slate-600 sm:text-base">
   114	            Choose a faster package path, let AI narrow decisions, or build the

   116	          </p>

   121
